- **External catalyst forcing affect through the defense.** On the rare occasions where grief or terror has been sharp enough and sudden enough to bypass intellectualization—Jean's deaths, certain of Bobby's crises, his father's mortality—he has produced moments of genuinely felt emotion in relational presence, and those moments have functioned as repair currency for the people who witnessed them. They are valuable in part because they are scarce.

What he cannot do, and has never demonstrated the capacity to do across sixty years: **structural moral repair by genuinely metabolizing harm, accepting unearned dependency on the wronged party's mercy, and rebuilding trust on their timeline rather than his.** The Krakoan-era execution by his peers, and his replacement by an earlier-resurrection Hank, is the in-universe verdict on this incapacity. The system around him concluded that he could not be repaired into. It is a brutal conclusion and the evidence supports it.

---

## 6.6 Intimacy and Dependency

Romantic intimacy in Hank's life has been **real, recurrent, and consistently truncated at a specific threshold.** The pattern:

- **Vera Cantor** (Defenders / early adult). Pre-fur courtship, librarian, intellectual peer. The relationship survives Hank's verbal performance because Vera reads him as charmingly bookish rather than defended. It does not survive the transformation; she is not equipped for the new body or the new life.
- **Trish Tilby** (X-Factor era through the secondary mutation). The most fully documented adult romance in the record. Trish is a television journalist—a woman who lives professionally in publics, the very domain Hank distrusts—and the relationship works precisely because she translates between his interior and his hostile outer world. It fails at the threshold of the secondary mutation: when the body crosses from blue-furred-but-recognizable into something more bestial, she does not stay. The breakup is observable in the record as one of his **load-bearing wounds**. It confirms, in the most personal possible register, the childhood thesis that the body is the variable. He has not had a comparably deep documented romance since.
- **Abigail Brand** (Astonishing X-Men into Krakoa). Operational-intellectual peer; SWORD director; a woman as defended as he is. The relationship reads as two armored people leaning the armor against each other rather than disclosing under it. It is functional, occasionally tender, and *structurally non-threatening to either party's defenses*. Telling, in what it does not require him to do.
- Various transient or unconsummated entanglements with figures who matched fragments of him but not the whole.

The pattern: **he can sustain intimacy with women who can tolerate the body and the verbal performance simultaneously, and he loses them at the point where one or the other proves unsustainable.** He has not, in canon, formed a long-stable cohabiting partnership of the kind his friend Reed Richards has with Sue or even the chaotic durability of Logan's various bonds. The wound channel from Trish onward shows him **avoiding the threshold rather than testing it again.**

The Simon Williams friendship deserves separate treatment because it is the **most relationally important non-familial bond** in his life. With Wonder Man during the Avengers years and afterward, Hank produced something he has produced with no one else: sustained, demonstrative, physically affectionate non-romantic intimacy. They roomed together. They went to the opera together. They appeared on television together. The bond was so visible that the readership has read it as romantic for decades, and the in-universe characters frequently teased it; Hank's own public coming-out and retraction in the New X-Men era is *partially legible as commentary on this very perception.* Whatever its precise valence—the canon underdetermines it—the Wonder Man bond is the **single relationship in which Hank permitted himself sustained, unguarded delight in another person's company.** Its gradual attenuation across decades, as Simon's own life shifted, is a quiet loss in the record that Hank has never overtly grieved and that may account for some of the increased brittleness of his later humor.

Dependency, finally: **he does not ask for help.** Across sixty years the record contains vanishingly few instances of Hank McCoy initiating a request for emotional support. He receives it when offered (Bobby in particular has volunteered it many times) and he is grateful in the receiving. He does not *seek* it. This is the avoidant pole of the split working model expressing itself in the most personal possible domain: the lesson that publics are hostile generalized, over decades, into the operational rule that *one does not put one's interior into anyone's hands without overwhelming reason*. Even with his vetted inner circle the disclosure tends to be retrospective—he tells Bobby about the crisis after he has solved it—rather than concurrent.

The cost of this pattern is structural: **he has no relational mechanism for being talked out of a bad decision before he makes it.** The peers who might have caught him have not been given the access in time. The time-travel decision, the Krakoa decisions—each was made in a small private room of his own mind where no one else was admitted. He did not depend on anyone for the decision. He could not be depended on to consult. The lack of dependency is not strength here. It is the *operational precondition* for the betrayals catalogued above.

---

## 6.7 The Relational Template, Repeated

Across every relationship in Hank's life—familial, romantic, fraternal, professional, adversarial—the same template repeats with variations:

1. **Encounter under verbal cover.** The other party meets the performance, not yet the person.
2. **Sustained observation through the cover.** He assesses, over time, whether they are safe to be partially seen by.
3. **Gradual register-shift toward plain speech** with those who pass. The shift is the relationship's actual content.
4. **Operational interdependence** with a vanishing few, in shared work.
5. **Withholding of full interior** even at the deepest stage—a residual cordon, never lifted with any party in the record.
6. **Unilateral decision-making in crisis** that bypasses the relationship's collaborative norms.
7. **Verbal repair offered post hoc**, conflating explanation with apology.
8. **Slow erosion or sudden rupture** depending on whether the partner can metabolize the unilateralism.

The template is recognizable in his bond with Xavier (mentor he eventually surpassed and unilateralized against); with Bobby (lifelong friend repeatedly withheld from); with Jean (intimate intellectual peer protected by curation of information); with Wonder Man (the relationship that came closest to escaping the template, and the record's lone partial exception); with Trish (the romance that failed at the bodily threshold); with Brand (the romance that survived by not testing the threshold); with the X-Men collectively (the institutional bond he repeatedly betrayed in their interest as he calculated it); with Cyclops (the brother-in-arms gradually ratcheted into enemy by accumulated unilateralisms); with his own resurrected earlier self (the relationship the system substituted when his template's terminal failure had become unmanageable).

The template's first instantiation is visible in the seventeen-year-old who quoted Byron to deflect a question about his feet. The template's terminal instantiation is visible in the man whose closest peers killed him and replaced him with a copy. **It is the same template throughout.** What changed is not the structure but the load it was asked to carry, and the consequent escalation of its defensive features into the unilateralisms that exhausted the patience of every relational partner he had. The tragedy here, as elsewhere in the dossier, is that the relational instrument that bought a frightened gigantic-handed child his way back into the social world was the same instrument that eventually severed him from it.


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION: DEFENSES & COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS

*Subject: McCoy, Henry Philip. The architecture of self-protection, ranked, instrumented, and traced longitudinally across six decades of observable behavior.*

---

## Preface: Why This Section Is the Whole File in Miniature

If one wanted to predict every major life decision Hank McCoy has made — the serum in 1972, the Avengers cocktail circuit, the staged coming-out, the Endangered Species pilgrimage to monsters, the time-travel of the original five, the Krakoan black-ops — one would not need biography. One would need only the defensive stack, because the stack *is* the man. McCoy's biography is what happens when an exceptionally elaborate and high-functioning defensive architecture, originally built around a single early wound (a visible body shamed in childhood), is given six decades, a genius-tier cognitive engine, and progressively heavier moral loads to carry.

This section maps that architecture floor by floor. We rank by primitiveness (Vaillant's hierarchy is the working frame: mature → neurotic → immature → primitive/psychotic). McCoy's stack is unusual in two respects: (a) it sits *very high* on the maturity axis for most of his life, which is what allows his decompensation to be so slow and so plausible; and (b) the *mature* defenses are themselves what eventually do the damage, because they over-perform. He is not destroyed by his primitive defenses. He is destroyed by his elite ones.

---

## I. MATURE DEFENSES (Vaillant Tier IV) — The Public Architecture

These four are the defenses he leads with, the ones his teammates see, the ones he would name if asked. They are real, they have produced enormous good, and they are also — under sustained pressure — the load-bearing walls that crack last and most catastrophically.

### 1. Sublimation — *the engine*

The conversion of unacceptable drive into socially valuable output. In McCoy this is industrial-scale. Shame at the body becomes ten thousand lab-hours; helplessness in the face of anti-mutant violence becomes vaccines, cures, gene-mapping; grief over Jean becomes another paper, another machine. Endangered Species is sublimation visible from orbit: the entire species' sterility is converted into a personal globe-trotting research program. He does not sit shiva. He goes to Sinister.

Behavioral signatures: the thirty-hour bench stretch; the refusal to take leave after losses (Cyclops noting, in multiple eras, that Hank's bereavement response is to ask for harder assignments); the lab as physical sanctuary; the way he greets crisis news with a tightened jaw and an immediate move toward equipment. Sublimation in McCoy is so effective that it has obscured, from him and from his peers, how much affect was never processed in the first place. The output substitutes for the metabolism.

### 2. Humor — *the lubricant*

Vaillant ranks humor at the apex of mature defense. McCoy uses it constantly, in three distinct registers:

- **Self-deprecating somatic humor.** The "bouncing blue beast" line and its thousand variants. Function: pre-empt the observer. If he names the body first, no one else's naming can wound him. This is *prophylactic* humor — he is jumping into the joke before the joke can be made about him, a behavioral fossil from the schoolyard.
- **Erudite-incongruity humor.** Quoting Wilde or Keats while breaking a Sentinel's arm; addressing a teammate mid-firefight as "dear fellow." Function: assert the dissonance between body and mind so loudly that the audience cannot collapse the two.
- **Dry clinical humor.** "The doctor must occasionally consent to be patient." Function: distance from his own physical and emotional states by reframing them as case material.

Longitudinal trend: through the 70s–90s humor is *warm*. From Decimation forward it acquires an edge — sharper, more sardonic, sometimes openly hostile (his exchanges with Cyclops in *Schism* and after). The thinning of warmth in the humor is one of the earliest and most reliable telemetry signals that the stack is degrading.

### 3. Anticipation — *the planner*

He pre-experiences difficulty in order to absorb it. He runs simulations, drafts contingencies, gamesplans threats. In his Avengers years this looks like preparation; in his X-Men years it looks like protocol; in his Krakoan years it metastasizes into pre-emption — *I will neutralize the Terra Verde situation before it can become a situation*. Anticipation, when it loses its boundary against unilateralism, becomes the rationale for acting on futures only he has modeled.

### 4. Altruism — *the vocation*

Genuine. Not performance. The teaching at the Jean Grey School, the open clinic for depowered mutants, the willingness to risk his own body in every self-experiment so no one else has to. This is the defense most easily mistaken for an unmotivated virtue; it is in fact load-bearing for the self-image (*I am useful, therefore the body is forgiven*). When altruism is fused this tightly to self-image, it stops functioning as service to the other and starts functioning as service to the self-as-savior. That fusion is the trapdoor under late-period Hank.

---

## II. NEUROTIC DEFENSES (Tier III) — The Working Middle

These are the defenses he uses every day, all day, that are mostly invisible to him because they feel like personality. They are the texture of how he moves through the world.

### 5. Intellectualization — *pathognomonic*

The single most diagnostic item in the entire file. Affect arrives, and is immediately translated upward into a register of abstraction, citation, taxonomy, or technical description. He does not say *I am frightened*; he says *the adrenal response is, predictably, unhelpful here*. He does not say *I miss her*; he constructs a sentence whose architecture requires three subordinate clauses and a Latin tag, and the missing arrives encrypted inside the grammar.

Behavioral markers, granular:
- **Lexical altitude index.** Word-frequency in his dialogue trends *upward* under stress. Most humans simplify their vocabulary when frightened; McCoy elaborates it. This inversion is the cleanest single behavioral biomarker in the file.
- **Latin/Greek tagging.** Density of classical reference correlates positively with proximity to grief or fear.
- **Clinical third person.** Under acute personal threat ("the patient presents with…", "the specimen appears…") he refers to himself as case material.
- **Question deflection through definition.** Asked how he feels: returns the etymology of the word "feel."

Cost: emotional data arrives at consciousness late, encoded, and often misrouted. By the time he knows he is angry, he has already acted on it; by the time he knows he is afraid, the fear has already shaped a decision he believes he made on the merits.

### 6. Isolation of Affect — *the firewall*

A closely related defense, but distinct: the *separation* of cognition from the feeling that should accompany it. He can describe his own dying body in *All-New X-Men* without his voice changing. He can recount what he did to Colossus during the Krakoa years in a flat expository register. The information is intact. The feeling-tone has been disengaged.

This is the defense that fails most consequentially in late period. The ethical brake in a healthy adult is *affective* — guilt, shame, dread — not purely logical. When affect is isolated from cognition, the brake stops engaging because the signal cannot reach the pedal. He can think *this is wrong* and continue, because the thought is not accompanied by the somatic alarm that would normally stop the body.

### 7. Rationalization — *the engine that destroys him*

Hank's rationalizations are not the lazy ones of an ordinary person ("I deserved it," "they had it coming"). They are *fully argued ethical proofs* with named premises and rigorous derivations. The time-travel of the original five is presented with utilitarian calculus. The Krakoan assassinations come with a doctrine. The Endangered Species deals with Sinister are accompanied by an internally consistent triage framework.

The pathology is not the *quality* of the argument; the pathology is that the argument is always *post-hoc* and the conclusion was foregone. He decides; then the reasoning faculty, which is enormous, dresses the decision in robes. Because the robes are so well-tailored — and because he is genuinely the most articulate person in most rooms — no one, including himself, can easily distinguish a McCoy rationalization from a McCoy reason. His teammates have to fall back on the dumb but accurate heuristic: *if Hank is being unusually eloquent about why a hard thing is necessary, the hard thing is probably wrong*.

### 8. Reaction Formation — *the dressing gown*

The conversion of an unacceptable impulse or self-perception into its opposite, behaviorally. As his body becomes more bestial — secondary mutation's feline drift, the slit pupils, the mane, the audible purr — his presentation becomes *more* cultured, not less. He sources better tailoring, quotes more poetry, plays more chess, takes up more obscure instruments, builds a more elaborate vocabulary. The opera box appearances are densest in the periods when his somatic dysphoria is most acute. The dressing gown over the fur is reaction formation made visible.

### 9. Displacement — *minor but present*

Frustration with Cyclops in *Schism* and after gets displaced onto policy disagreements about pedagogy. Anger at himself for Endangered Species gets displaced onto the geneticists he was forced to consort with. The displacement is mild compared to his other defenses and rarely lasts long, because intellectualization soon reclaims the affect and dissolves it into analysis.

### 10. Undoing — *trace*

Mostly visible in his pattern of *fixing* what he has broken: the elaborate aftercare he provides teammates he has previously misjudged or harmed, the gestures of restitution toward those wronged in operations he sanctioned. Limited efficacy; the undone act remains done.

---

## III. IMMATURE DEFENSES (Tier II) — The Late-Period Leakage

McCoy spent forty years not using these. Their appearance in the canon, from roughly Endangered Species onward, is itself the clinical event.

### 11. Omnipotent Control / Compensatory Grandiosity

Not present in early Hank. *Strongly* present in late Hank. The conviction that he can — and therefore must — personally manage outcomes at species scale. Krakoan-era intelligence chiefdom is omnipotent control formalized into a job description. The decision to time-pull the original five is omnipotent control across the temporal axis.

The behavioral signature: the *shrinking circle* of who is consulted before he acts. In 1980 he consults the team. In 2000 he consults Xavier. In 2012 he consults himself and announces. In 2020 he doesn't even announce until the operation is complete.

### 12. Devaluation

Late-period only, and selective. He develops the habit of subtly downgrading the intellectual or moral standing of anyone who opposes his current operation. Cyclops, post-Schism, is no longer a peer disagreed with but a man whose judgment is publicly characterized as compromised. Teammates who object to Krakoan methods are framed (in his internal logic, leaking into his speech) as insufficiently realistic, insufficiently mature, insufficiently educated in the actual stakes. Devaluation is how the rationalization engine pre-clears the social field of inconvenient witnesses.

### 13. Idealization (of self-as-instrument)

He does not idealize others; he idealizes the *version of himself* required by the operation. The McCoy who must do the hard thing is framed (to himself) as the only one with the requisite intelligence, conscience, and courage to bear the cost. This is the precise mechanism by which compensatory narcissism stabilizes itself: not by claiming to be great in general, but by being indispensable in particular.

### 14. Acting Out — *rare, telling*

Largely absent — he is famously controlled. But there are isolated late-period episodes (physical confrontations he could have de-escalated, surgical decisions made faster than the situation required) that read as affect leaking past the firewall and discharging through the body, which had been the original site of the wound. When McCoy acts out, it is almost always *somatic*: the hand moves, the claw extends, before the mind has consented. That the body would be the leak-point is consistent with the body being the buried problem.

### 15. Passive Aggression — *minor*

Visible mostly in his late-period correspondence and committee behavior: agreement followed by inaction, deferred replies, ostensible cooperation that quietly fails to materialize. The defense is not characteristic, but its appearance — in a man who was, for decades, scrupulously direct — is data.

---

## IV. PRIMITIVE DEFENSES (Tier I) — Largely Absent, Critical Where Present

McCoy does not split, project, deny psychotically, or fragment. He is not borderline-organized. The near-absence of Tier I defenses is what made his decompensation so difficult to see coming — clinicians and teammates were watching for the wrong picture.

### 16. Denial — *narrow but lethal*

Not global denial. Specific, focal denial of one proposition: *I am becoming what I have opposed*. The proposition is presented to him repeatedly across late period — by Bobby, by Logan, by Storm, by his own reflection — and is each time refused, not by argument but by the simple non-registration of the data. This focal denial is the keystone of the rationalization arch; remove it and the whole structure collapses, which is precisely why it cannot be removed from the inside.

### 17. Splitting — *traces, late*

Not characteristic. But the late-period framing of Cyclops as essentially-bad and himself-and-his-faction as essentially-correct shows splitting's grammar entering speech that previously held complexity. Brief, partial, and not characterologic — but present.

---

## V. POSITIVE COMPENSATORY LEDGER

Distinct from defenses: the substantive *constructions* he has built atop the defensive base. These are real-world goods produced by the architecture.

- **Scientific contribution.** Genuine, sustained, field-shaping work in mutant genetics, biochemistry, and biophysics. Many lives saved, many fields advanced. Not merely sublimation residue; *art*.
- **Teaching vocation.** The Jean Grey School faculty role. He is, by repeated testimony of his students, a transformative pedagogue. The patience he extends to a struggling teenager is the patience he could never extend to himself.
- **Friendship capacity.** The Drake bond, the Wonder Man bond, the Jean bond — each measured in decades, each surviving ruptures that would have ended ordinary friendships. The friendships are the part of him the defensive architecture did not have to manufacture; they grew in the soil his parents provided.
- **Physical courage.** Unflinching, unbroken across sixty years. He has never run from a fight he believed needed fighting, and the willingness to be the first body in the door is not posture.
- **Ethical framing of technical questions.** He is, for most of his career, the conscience of every lab he enters. He insists on consent protocols, harm-reduction frames, refusal of weapons applications. This is genuine virtue, and it makes the late-period collapse of those same principles unbearable to watch.
- **Romantic tenderness.** With Vera, with Trish, with Abigail Brand — the record shows real intimate capacity. He is a *good* partner inside the bounds his body allows others to tolerate, and the wound when partners cannot tolerate is borne with grace, not retaliation.

---

## VI. NEGATIVE COMPENSATORY LEDGER

The dark side of the same architecture.

- **The savior posture.** *I alone can compute this.* The structural endpoint of altruism fused to self-image.
- **Epistemic arrogance under pressure.** Inability to update when peers disagree, precisely when stakes are highest.
- **Instrumentation of allies.** The Colossus resurrection abuses; the deployment of teammates as assets in operations they had not consented to. The most damning items on the file.
- **The eloquence-as-armor problem.** His articulate command of ethical language makes him *harder* to correct than a less articulate person would be, because he can always out-argue the objector in real time. The asymmetry of rhetorical firepower is itself a moral hazard, and he has not, in sixty years, learned to handicap himself for it.
- **Performance fatigue costs paid by intimates.** Partners and close friends report (in the record's various private exchanges) the sense of being addressed by a *performance* of McCoy even in unguarded moments. The defensive stack does not switch off; intimates live with the always-on version.
- **Body-image displacement onto cultural signaling.** The dressing gown / opera / Wilde quotations are not free goods. They burn cycles, they cost money, they distance him from anyone uninterested in or unimpressed by the signal. The reaction formation has a social tax he pays daily.

---

## VII. THE STACK UNDER LOAD — Stage-by-Stage Decompensation

The defenses do not all fail at once. They fail in a characteristic order, and the order is the prognostic key.

**Stage 1 — Verbal Elevation.** Lexical altitude rises. Latin density rises. Humor sharpens but remains within his usual range. *Sublimation, humor, intellectualization* are all functioning normally and absorbing the load. This is daily-baseline McCoy and most of his life.

**Stage 2 — Withdrawal Into Sublimation.** Sleep hours drop. Lab hours expand. Social contact narrows to the operationally necessary. Meals taken at the bench. He becomes harder to reach. *Anticipation* begins to widen its scope beyond the proximate. This is McCoy during any significant crisis, and it is mostly healthy.

**Stage 3 — Isolation of Affect Becomes Total.** He stops mentioning feelings even ironically. Clinical third-person increases. Friends report a *flatness* under the wit. The firewall has hardened. The ethical brake is now operating on logic alone, without affective backup. This stage is observable in late Decimation and again in the early Krakoa period.

**Stage 4 — Rationalization Takes The Wheel.** A decision is made, swiftly, and is then encased in an elegant ethical proof. Consultation circle shrinks. Devaluation of objectors begins. Focal denial of the proposition *I am becoming what I oppose* hardens into reflex. This is the time-travel decision; this is the Terra Verde operation; this is the Colossus instrumentation.

**Stage 5 — The Body Leaks.** Acting-out increments. The claw extends a beat early. The voice drops half an octave in committee. The reaction formation strains visibly — the dressing gown sits poorly on a body now visibly disinhibited. This is McCoy at the end of his Krakoan tenure, and it is the stage at which his peers finally moved against him.

There is no Stage 6 because there is no observed McCoy past Stage 5 in his own person. The system around him intervened. His replacement was an *earlier* version of himself — the architecture rolled back to a point before Stage 4 had become characterologic. This is the closest thing in the record to a clinical verdict on which stage was the recoverable one.

---

## VIII. Concluding Observation

The cruelty of McCoy's defensive structure is that *it was never wrong on its own terms*. Each defense did what it was built to do. Sublimation produced cures. Humor kept the team morale buoyant for forty years. Intellectualization made him the best diagnostician on three teams. Anticipation saved lives. Altruism built a school. Reaction formation gave the world an extraordinary aesthete. These are not malfunctions. These are *successes*, sustained at a level few human nervous systems could match.

What the file shows is that even an elite defensive stack has a load ceiling, and that when the loads exceed the ceiling — Decimation, Schism, terminal diagnosis, Krakoa — the failure mode of a *mature* stack is not regression to immature defense. It is the *over-performance* of the mature defenses themselves: sublimation that builds the wrong cure, anticipation that authorizes pre-emption, humor that turns acid, altruism that fuses to the self until it cannot tell the other from the self, rationalization that retains all its rigor while losing its referent.

He was not undone by his weaknesses. He was undone by his strengths, applied past the point where any human conscience could keep up with them. The dossier's deepest finding is structural and not moral: *a defensive architecture this good is a moral hazard in proportion to how good it is.* McCoy is the canonical case. The seventeen-year-old who quoted Byron to deflect a question about his feet had, in the same gesture, installed the operating system that, sixty years later, would let him green-light an assassination without his pulse changing.

— UATU. End of section.


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# LONGITUDINAL PSYCHOLOGICAL PROFILE: HENRY PHILIP McCOY

*Decade-by-decade clinical mapping. Affect regulation, cognitive style, and self-concept tracked across the published record, 1963–present, with the developmental logic that connects each phase to the next.*

---

## Preamble: The Three Axes

This file tracks three variables through time, because no one of them alone captures the trajectory:

1. **Affect regulation** — the speed, accuracy, and cost of his emotional throttling. Across his life this is his most stable-*looking* function and his most quietly deteriorating one. He never loses control; he loses *contact*.
2. **Cognitive style** — the shape of his thinking: hyper-associative, polymathic, analogizing across domains, with a characteristic verbal compression he uses as both signal and shield. The substance of the cognition is durable across sixty years; what changes is its *relationship to other people's cognition*, which contracts.
3. **Self-concept** — the working answer to "what am I?" The answer migrates: from *defective body redeemed by exceptional mind*, through *celebrated mind housed in interesting body*, to *indispensable mind constrained by failing body*, and finally to *the only mind willing to do what must be done*. Each migration is a defensive maneuver, and each costs him a piece of the previous self.

The decade markers below are imprecise by design — Marvel time compresses — but they map cleanly onto the publication eras and the discrete bodily transformations that punctuate his life.

---

## Phase I — Adolescence into Early Adulthood: The Acrobat-Scholar (1963 era / X-Men vol. 1)

**Self-concept.** The defining fact of the early McCoy is that his mutation was *visible from birth*, which means he never had a pre-mutant identity to mourn. There is no "before." There is only the lifelong project of *justifying the body by appending things to it*: a high school football career stapled onto the freakish feet; a graduate-level vocabulary stapled onto the prehensile limbs; a Xavier-vetted heroic identity stapled onto a teenager whose proportions had already been a small-town spectacle for sixteen years. The self-concept at this stage is *additive and compensatory*: the body is the given, everything else is the answer. He is, in his own private accounting, an apology with abilities.

This produces the most diagnostic early tic in the record: the polysyllable mid-acrobatics. Hank, in the original Lee/Kirby issues, *narrates his own combat* in a register two registers above his teammates. Bobby Drake calls it showing off; it is in fact a near-textbook *display of compensatory mastery*. The verbalization runs concurrent with the physical performance because both are simultaneously on trial. He is not choosing between mind and body in adolescence; he is performing them in parallel, lest the audience notice that the body is the original problem.

**Affect regulation.** Quite good for an adolescent, and almost suspiciously frictionless. He does not have the moodiness of Bobby, the smolder of Scott, the grief-saturation of Warren-post-wing-loss. He presents *cheerful*, *team-positive*, *easily redirected*. This is not depth — it is early-stage intellectualization functioning at full throttle. Affect is being routed through cognition before it can register as affect. He metabolizes Xavier's lectures with hungry uptake because the school is *the first environment in his life that has a use for the whole specimen*. The relief of being a recognized intellect among peers who are themselves anomalous is not, at this stage, processed as relief — it is processed as opportunity. The feeling will not be available to him as a feeling until much later, in elegiac reference, after some of those peers are dead.

**Cognitive style.** Already hyper-associative; already drawn to biology over engineering (a clue: he wants to understand *life*, his own most). Already showing the tell that will define him at sixty: when asked a question, he answers a more interesting adjacent question. Already exhibiting the auto-didact's vice — he reads ahead of his teachers and trusts his own synthesis more than the syllabus's. This is harmless in a teenager. The structure that will later let him out-reason his own ethical brakes is the same structure that lets him, at seventeen, correct a graduate student in passing.

**Net Phase I read.** A well-defended, well-loved, visibly different child has constructed an exit ramp from shame via two parallel highways — athletic prowess and intellectual prowess — and has the unusual luck of arriving at an institution that values both. The defenses are working. They are *too* good; nothing is being processed at depth because nothing has to be. The bill comes due later.

---

## Phase II — The First Transformation and the Solo Year (Amazing Adventures era, early 1970s)

**Self-concept fracture and re-set.** This is the first earthquake. Hank, working at Brand Corporation as a young geneticist, drinks his own mutagenic catalyst to disguise himself and is trapped first in a gray-furred feral state, then settling to blue. The diagnostic feature is not the transformation. It is *that he did it to himself*. The pattern — self as primary experimental subject — is set here for life. He will never again trust another body to bear the risk of his curiosity.

The self-concept rewrites under duress. The compensatory architecture of Phase I was *body-as-given, mind-as-answer*. He has now *altered* the given. This is, psychologically, a paradoxical mastery move: by transforming the body further from human, he claims authorship of it. The shame in Phase I was that he had not chosen the body; now he has, sort of, chosen this one. The cost of the move is buried under its short-term relief, and will not be visible until the secondary mutation thirty publication-years later, when the body changes *without his consent again* and the old wound is found to have been merely papered over.

**Affect regulation under acute crisis.** The Brand-era arc shows the only sustained period in his life of *unregulated affect*: the feral phase, the loss of verbal control, the post-transformation aggression. It is brief. He reins it in. But the experience leaves a residue — a permanent knowledge that *the verbal man is removable*, that the polysyllabic self is a thin film over something with teeth. Every later joke about the beast within is informed by the fact that he has met it. This is part of why his humor about his appearance is so durable: it is gallows humor from someone who has seen the gallows.

**Cognitive style.** Sharpens here in a specific direction: he becomes a *practicing* scientist rather than a precocious student. He acquires the lab-bench habits — the 30-hour work cycles, the willingness to be his own control group, the impatience with slower minds — that will define his professional life. The auto-didactic confidence of Phase I matures into actual research competence and, problematically, the certainty that *he is the appropriate person to make the call* on his own experiments. Institutional review processes do not bind him because he is, in his own framing, the most qualified reviewer in the room. This is locally true and globally dangerous.

---

## Phase III — The Avengers Decade: Maximal Extroversion (mid-1970s into early 1980s)

**Self-concept at peak integration.** This is the *only sustained period* in the record where Hank's self-concept is not primarily compensatory. The Avengers tenure provides him an audience — high society, the press, fellow capes who are themselves spectacular — for whom *the blue fur is an asset rather than a stigma*. He is, briefly, glamorous. The body has stopped being an apology and started being a costume. He responds the way a man released from a long held-in breath responds: he expands.

This is the McCoy of the opera box, the tuxedo, the cocktail repartee, the Wonder Man friendship, the Vera Cantor romance. It is also the only period when the *register of his speech matches the register of his life*. In Phase I the polysyllables were over-armor for an adolescent; here they fit a man who is genuinely moving through cultured rooms. The performance and the reality have, briefly, converged. He will later attempt to reconstruct this convergence at the Jean Grey School and again, more darkly, in Krakoan parlors, and never quite manage it.

**Affect regulation.** *Best in show* across his life. Wide bandwidth, slow refractory period, accurate emotional read of others, available warmth, available irritation, available pleasure. The intellectualization is still running but it is not the only channel — he is also *feeling* things in real time and acting on them. The friendship with Wonder Man is the index case: it is mutual, durable, characterological, founded on actual emotional reciprocity rather than on co-operational professionalism. He has, by this point, the capacity to love a friend without converting the love into a project.

**Cognitive style.** Still polymathic, but applied in lower-stakes registers — engineering puzzles in service of the Avengers, the occasional consult, the wit deployed for pleasure rather than for self-defense. The cognition is *at play*, which is the only time in his life it is meaningfully at play. He writes well in this period — the few in-fiction articles and letters we see are looser, more humorous, less embattled. He has time to be amused.

**Why this matters longitudinally.** Every later phase is, in part, an unsuccessful attempt to recover this baseline. He keeps trying to be the Avengers-era Hank in increasingly inhospitable conditions. The cocktail-party verbal repertoire persists into the Krakoan war rooms, where it has curdled into something else, but the syntactic fingerprints are the same. He is, in part, mourning this version of himself for the next forty years.

---

## Phase IV — Return to the X-Front: X-Factor and the Re-Darkening (late 1980s)

**Self-concept under retraction.** The original five reunite under the false flag of being mutant hunters — the premise itself is a moral pretzel — and Hank's self-concept contracts back from *celebrity intellectual* to *covert minority operative*. The Avengers-era expansiveness is rolled back; he is again managing a public that wants him dead. The shame doesn't return as shame; it returns as a slightly louder version of the old performance — more jokes, more polysyllables, more visible enjoyment of his own erudition. The volume increase is the tell.

**Affect regulation, first cracks.** The Infectia event — temporary loss of intellect in exchange for greater bestiality — is the first time the *intellect-versus-animal* dialectic gets explicit narrative treatment. He recovers, but the encounter writes a new file into the system: *the mind is not guaranteed*. Affect regulation in this period begins to show a specific brittleness — he is fine until he is asked about his appearance or his cognition, at which point the response is fractionally over-fast and fractionally over-witty. The latency of the joke shortens. A joke arriving too fast is a defense arriving with the alarm still ringing.

**Cognitive style.** Hardens into *the team's resident scientist* in a way it had not been formalized before. The role gives him both a slot to occupy and a justification for his characteristic isolation in the lab. He begins, in this period, to take on the procedural rhythm — long lab cycles, brief field excursions, return to the lab — that will be the structural pattern of his life. The cognition turns more applied, less ludic.

---

## Phase V — The 1990s into Early 2000s: Scientist-Ethicist, Legacy Virus, Conscience-Of-The-Team

**Self-concept as moral anchor.** This is the period in which Hank settles, formally, into the role he will hold for the next decade: *the conscience of the X-Men*. Legacy Virus research, ethical consultation on team operations, the public face when nuance is required. The self-concept stabilizes around *the one who thinks carefully about hard things on behalf of those who can't or won't*. This is a noble self-image and, for a long time, an accurate one. It is also, in the longer view, the seed crystal of the late-period catastrophe — because once you accept that you are the team's ethicist, the institutional incentive against deferring to consensus is suddenly considerable. *Why poll the room when you are the room's polled expert?*

**Affect regulation, mid-life pattern.** The Legacy Virus work — months and years of failure, mutant deaths he could not prevent — produces what is structurally a dysthymic undertow that he metabolizes by working harder. The pattern of *grief → sublimation → output* is now mature and effectively invisible. He looks, to teammates and the reader, like he is *coping well*. He is coping by *not coping* — by routing the entire affect stream into the lab. This is highly adaptive in the short term and disastrous in the long because the practice of *not feeling the loss* eventually becomes the practice of *not feeling the harm one's own decisions cause*. The muscle that should have caught his late-period drift is the muscle he was busy not exercising in this period.

**Cognitive style.** Reaches what is probably its functional peak. The work is hard, the work is real, the conclusions matter, and he is in dialogue with peers he respects (Moira MacTaggert above all, until her arc complicates that). The polymathic synthesis is being deployed against the worst biological problem in the X-Men's history and is, in its way, the most productive cognition of his life. The vice in the style — the analogizing from domain to domain — is *exactly the asset* in this kind of synthetic biology, so the vice is rewarded, which makes it deeper.

---

## Phase VI — The Secondary Mutation: Dysmorphia Returns (Morrison's New X-Men, early 2000s)

**Self-concept earthquake, second iteration.** The leonine drift — paws, fangs, slit pupils, mane, audible purring under load — is the second time his body has remade itself, but the *first* time since the Brand-era self-experiment that the remaking happened *without his consent*. The Phase II solution — *I chose this body* — no longer applies. The original Phase I shame is therefore *reactivated unmitigated*: he is once again being given a body he did not ask for.

The response is twofold and revealing. First, the *reaction formation* spikes: more cultured presentation, more Wilde, more Shakespeare, more dressing gown, more opera, as if to outrun the felinity with footnotes. Second, the *public self-staging* — most famously the come-out-and-recant gambit about being gay, framed as a provocation against identity policing. The maneuver is diagnostic: under acute identity disruption, his response is to *stage his own identity* as a rhetorical weapon, to make the question of *what he is* into a problem the public has rather than a problem he has. This is brilliantly defended and emotionally evasive in roughly equal measure. He has externalized the dysmorphia by making it a public-discourse object.

**Affect regulation.** Holds, but at higher cost. The relationship with Trish Tilby — already long-running, already strained by his appearance through prior iterations — does not survive this transformation. The breakup wound is processed, predictably, through the lab and the lectern. He does not present as grieving. He presents as busy.

**Cognitive style.** The Morrison-era McCoy is, intellectually, a virtuoso — the team's interface with cutting-edge weirdness (Sublime, U-Men, Cassandra Nova-tier threats). The cognition is at full operational stretch. But this is also when one can begin to see the *signature late-period vice* in embryo: he begins to make calls — research calls, strategic calls — and *narrate them as if no other call were possible*. The Morrison era is too short for this to do damage. The pattern is filed for use.

---

## Phase VII — Decimation and Endangered Species: The First Moral Wound (mid-to-late 2000s)

**Self-concept under load it was not built for.** After M-Day, 90%+ of mutants are depowered. The X-Men's existential project — the survival of a people — is now a *species-extinction* problem. The team's resident scientist-ethicist is, by default, the man asked to fix it. The self-concept *inflates* under the demand: he is no longer *one of those who thinks carefully* but *the one who must solve this*. The shift from *participant ethicist* to *sole responsible mind* is enormous and largely invisible to him, because it happens by accretion of others' deference rather than by any decision on his part.

**The compromise.** In *Endangered Species*, he solicits help from every villainous geneticist alive — Sinister, the High Evolutionary, Dark Beast (his own mirror, which should have been a warning siren and instead became, characteristically, an interesting datum). He fails. The failure is, in his accounting, *the failure of the mind to solve the problem*, which lands directly on the load-bearing wall of his entire identity. The compensatory architecture from Phase I — *the mind redeems the body* — has now generalized into *the mind redeems the species*, and the mind has been found insufficient. This is the *first true moral injury* in the record: not the consorting with monsters per se, but his inability to convert the consorting into a successful outcome that would have retroactively justified it.

**Affect regulation, sustained crack.** He does not present as broken. He presents as *more compressed*. The humor thins. The polysyllables continue but begin to be deployed against rather than for his interlocutors — there is a faint edge of *I am the smartest person in this room and you should know it* that was absent in earlier phases. This is the beginning of the late-period drift: a small narcissistic spike, compensatory to the unmetabolized failure.

**Cognitive style.** Still excellent, still synthetic, but with a new quiet feature: *willingness to suspend ethical pre-screening* of which collaborations he will undertake. He has learned that he can work with Sinister without becoming Sinister. This is true. He has not learned that the ability to do so without becoming Sinister is *not the same thing* as the ability to do so without cost. The unmetabolized cost is what he carries forward into Schism.

---

## Phase VIII — Schism through the Jean Grey School: The Teacher Phase, with Undertow (early 2010s)

**Self-concept as restorative project.** Siding with Wolverine, founding the school, becoming faculty — Hank attempts, in this period, to reconstruct a self-concept around *teaching* the next generation rather than *saving* the current one. It is partially successful. The mentor identity is real, and the warmth he shows students (Idie, Broo especially) is real. The Phase III gregariousness flickers back in glimpses.

**The undertow.** But the alienation from Scott Summers is metastasizing under the surface, and the alienation is not really about Scott. It is about *Xavier's death* and the symbolic loss of the father-figure who modeled the *benevolent unilateralism* Hank is about to weaponize. Hank's rage at Scott is, in part, displaced grief about what the dream has become — and, in part, a projection of his own emergent willingness to act without consensus onto the man who already did. Scott becomes the carrier for the disowned future-Hank.

**Affect regulation.** The mentor role gives the affect somewhere to go that is not the lab — students require warmth, and warmth requires affect to be available, not isolated. So this period shows *partial re-engagement* of feeling. But it is selective. He is warm in the classroom; he is increasingly clipped in the war room. The compartmentalization tightens.

**Cognitive style.** Pedagogically excellent — broad, generous, contagious. Operationally, beginning to show the *I have already decided* posture in command settings. The two cognitive registers diverge: *teaching cognition* (open, exploratory) and *operational cognition* (closed, executive). Both are him; only one of them is being audited.

---

## Phase IX — The Time-Travel Decision: The Rubicon (mid-2010s)

**Self-concept under terminal framing.** He believes he is dying — the tertiary mutation presents as terminal cellular instability. The terminal framing is the *single most important variable* in his life, because it removes the long-time-horizon discipline that has, until now, kept his rationalization engine within the speed limit. *If I will not be here to be wrong about this, the cost of being wrong is bounded.* The reasoning is not made explicit in dialogue but is structurally legible: he calibrates *now* against *never*, and *never* wins.

The decision to retrieve the original five teenage X-Men from the past — to *force the present-day Scott Summers to face the children they once were* — is staged by Hank as a moral gambit. Every other voice in the room calls it reckless, monstrous, causally irresponsible. He proceeds. The diagnostic feature is not the decision itself; it is *his serene confidence in his right to make it*. He is making a call about the timeline, the lives of his teenage friends, and the autonomy of his teammates, and he is doing so *unilaterally*, *under terminal framing*, *with no peer review of the ethics*.

**This is the moment the OCP scaffolding from his childhood becomes formally narcissistic in operation.** Until this point, his unilateralism has been *opportunistic* (when others were absent, when speed required it). Now it becomes *principled*: he believes the others *would* stop him and that they *shouldn't get to*. The lack of *empathy for the teens being abducted* — they have no say in being taken from their own lives — is the cleanest narcissistic data point in the record.

**Affect regulation.** Calm. Eerily calm. The decision is made in the *register of considered reasoning*, not crisis. This is the affect-isolation pattern at its most dangerous: an act with enormous emotional weight, being executed with no internal emotional alarm. The brake that should have engaged is affective, and the affect has been routed elsewhere for forty years.

**Cognitive style.** *Airtight in form, hollow in audit.* The ethical reasoning he offers is internally consistent. It is also unfalsifiable from inside his own head, because he has no longer practiced the discipline of *modeling his interlocutors' objections as potentially correct*. Every objection is processed as data to be defeated, not as a possible signal that his model is wrong. This is the signature failure mode of late-period polymaths who have spent decades being right about things their peers were wrong about: the prior probability of *I am right and they are wrong* has been trained too high.

---

## Phase X — Krakoa: The Spymaster (late 2010s into early 2020s)

**Self-concept fully decompensated.** As head of intelligence for Krakoa, Hank presides over assassinations, coups, the toppling of Terra Verde, the abuse and serial resurrection of Piotr Rasputin. The self-concept has resolved into *the necessary monster*: he is the one who will do the unspeakable so that the rest of the mutants can keep their hands clean. This is the moral-injury endgame: *I have already crossed lines, therefore I am the appropriate person to keep crossing them, therefore the lines are not really lines*.

The Krakoan parlor manner — the dressing gown, the tea service, the Wilde — is now a *grotesque inversion* of the Avengers-era cultured ease. Same syntactic fingerprints, opposite function. In Phase III the manner expressed an integrated self; in Phase X it papers over a man who has decided that resurrection technology has rendered consent optional. The cocktail-party McCoy is being run on a corpse — the original ethical Hank — and the cocktail-party McCoy *does not notice*.

**Affect regulation in terminal mode.** Affect has been *fully* isolated from operational decision-making. He performs warmth, he performs irritation, he performs amusement; none of these performances appear to *constrain* what he is willing to do. The affective brake is no longer connected to the wheel. This is what makes the Krakoa-era McCoy frightening to read: there is no detectable internal cost to him for any of it. The cost is being paid in him; it is simply no longer accessible to him as feeling.

**Cognitive style as weapon.** The polymathic synthes


## Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

# PSYCHIATRIC ASSESSMENT & DIFFERENTIAL

*Subject: McCoy, Henry Philip. File-internal designation: BEAST/HPM. Assessment integrates sixty-plus years of observable behavior, speech samples, decisional record, and somatic data. No first-person clinical interview is or will be available; what follows is a behaviorally-derived formulation written to the standard of a forensic-grade longitudinal psychiatric workup.*

---

## 1. Framing the Diagnostic Problem

The first thing that must be said, because it is the thing that most often goes unsaid in casual readings of this subject: **Hank McCoy is not, on any axis, a textbook case of a single, clean disorder.** He does not present a primary mood disorder, a primary psychotic disorder, a substance use disorder, a paraphilia, a tic disorder, or an anxiety disorder meeting full criteria. He is, in the working language of the file, a *structurally high-functioning subject with a personality-level vulnerability that has decompensated under chronic and escalating stress into a recognizable late-life syndrome.*

That distinction matters operationally. Subjects of his type are routinely under-diagnosed for decades because their pathology is *productive* — it generates Nobel-grade work, saved lives, classroom teaching, friendship. Their decompensations, when they arrive, are read by laypeople as "moral failure" or "loss of nerve" rather than as the predictable failure mode of the original defensive architecture. The job of this section is to refuse both errors: to neither pathologize his virtues nor moralize his pathology.

The formulation below is layered: a personality-level chassis (the chronic substrate), a set of acquired syndromes (built on top of it across decades), an acute late-period decompensation (the visible crisis), and a careful differential listing of what he is *not* and the evidence ruling each alternative out.

---

## 2. Primary Formulation: Obsessive-Compulsive Personality, with Acquired Compensatory Narcissism, Layered Moral Injury, and Dysmorphic Undertow

### 2.1 Obsessive-Compulsive Personality (the chassis)

The single most accurate label for Hank's stable, decades-long, ego-syntonic baseline is **Obsessive-Compulsive Personality (OCP)** in the DSM sense (and the *anankastic* personality cluster in ICD parlance). This is the personality *style* — not the OCD anxiety disorder, which he does not have; he reports no intrusive ego-dystonic thoughts, performs no neutralizing rituals, exhibits no hand-washing, counting, checking, or symmetry behaviors. The conflation of these two entities by non-specialists has dogged readings of him for years and must be set aside here.

Criteria he meets, with behavioral citations:

- **Preoccupation with details, rules, lists, order, organization, or schedules to the extent that the major point of the activity is lost.** Observable in his lab protocols (the Brand Corporation work pre-transformation; the secondary-mutation lab notebooks; the Endangered Species methodology). His write-ups are meticulous to the point that collaborators have observed that the documentation often outweighs the experiment.
- **Perfectionism that interferes with task completion.** Visible repeatedly in his unwillingness to publish intermediate findings; his repeated rebuilding of equipment to specifications no team member can interpret as necessary; his iterative re-derivation of the cure for the Legacy Virus where he discarded passable solutions in favor of theoretically cleaner ones.
- **Excessive devotion to work and productivity to the exclusion of leisure activities and friendships.** The Avengers period is the *exception* that proves the rule — it is the only sustained stretch in which he behaves like a normal social animal. Across the X-Factor, X-Men, and Krakoan eras he reverts to 30-hour lab cycles and treats vacation as failure mode.
- **Over-conscientious, scrupulous, and inflexible about matters of morality, ethics, or values.** Pathognomonic. Hank does not have ethics; Hank *performs* ethics, continuously, in committee with himself, often aloud, frequently in formal philosophical vocabulary. His moralism is not occasional; it is the air he breathes.
- **Reluctance to delegate tasks or to work with others unless they submit to exactly his way of doing things.** Observe his repeated insistence on being the *sole* experimental subject. Observe his pattern across Endangered Species of consulting villainous geneticists *as data sources* rather than as collaborators — he extracts information and reserves the synthesis to himself.
- **Rigidity and stubbornness.** Documented across every major arc. Once Hank decides, Hank does not unwind the decision; he reinforces it.

He does *not* meet the miserly-with-money or hoarding criteria. So: a partial but unambiguous OCP picture, ego-syntonic, lifelong, with onset in adolescence or earlier.

**Etiology of the OCP chassis.** Standard etiology for OCP is heterogeneous — temperamental conscientiousness, modeling of high-standards parenting, anxiety-binding via control. Hank's case has an additional and *specific* etiologic loading: the visible congenital mutation. A child who learns by age four that the world will treat him as a spectacle has powerful incentive to develop a defensive structure organized around *control of presentation* — control of speech, control of intellect, control of output, control of moral standing. OCP is precisely the personality structure that delivers that control. It was, in his developmental context, *adaptive*. This matters because his pathology is not foreign to his virtue; it is the same structure viewed from different angles.

### 2.2 Acquired Compensatory Narcissism (the late overlay)

Early Hank does not present narcissistically. The teenage and young-adult record shows self-deprecation, team deference, a willingness to be the comic foil, no grandiose self-statements not tagged with irony. **Narcissistic features in this subject are acquired, not primary**, and they map onto the decades-long inflation of the compensatory architecture described in Section 3 of the workup.

By the late-period (post-Schism, into Krakoa), he meets functional thresholds on the following Narcissistic Personality criteria:

- **Grandiose sense of self-importance.** The time-travel decision is the cleanest single-action evidence: he believes his moral reading of the Cyclops situation is correct *against the unanimous objection of every peer*, and he acts on that belief at species-altering scale.
- **Belief that he is "special" and can only be understood by other high-status / high-intellect people.** Observable in his selective consultation pattern — he turns to Reed Richards, T'Challa, Doom, the High Evolutionary, Sinister, when consulting at all; he does not consult his actual teammates because, by Krakoa, he no longer believes they are operating at his level of analysis.
- **Sense of entitlement — unreasonable expectations of especially favorable treatment, or automatic compliance with his expectations.** The Krakoan X-Force record is essentially this criterion in operational form. He stands up an intelligence service, operates it outside Quiet Council oversight, and reacts to challenge as if oversight itself were the offense.
- **Interpersonal exploitation.** Most damningly, the serial death-and-resurrection of Colossus to extract intelligence — instrumentalization of a friend's body as a means.
- **Lack of empathy in specific contexts.** Not globally — he retains empathy for abstract populations (mutantkind, the depowered, the time-displaced as a class) — but in the operational moment, his empathy for the specific person his decision will injure goes offline. The teen O5 are stranded, traumatized, and lose years of their original timeline; he does not absorb this as harm done.

The clinical name for this is **compensatory** or **vulnerable narcissism transitioning to grandiose** under chronic role-inflation. The pattern is well-known: a person with a shame core who has spent decades being told he is exceptional eventually starts believing the press release at exactly the moment circumstances start demanding more of him than the press release can support. The structure inflates to fill the demand. Once inflated, it does not deflate gracefully.

It is critical to specify: this is **not** Narcissistic Personality Disorder as a primary, lifelong structure. It is a **secondary narcissistic decompensation of an OCP base**, occurring late, in response to specific stressors (Decimation, terminal diagnosis, the Krakoan power-vacuum), and reversible in principle if the stressors abated and the subject accepted intervention. He did not, and they did not, and so it didn't.

### 2.3 Moral Injury (the operative late-period concept)

This is not a DSM construct but it is the most clinically useful single frame for the post-2007 record. Moral Injury, as developed in the military-psychiatry literature (Litz, Shay), describes the syndrome that follows when a person *commits, witnesses, or fails to prevent acts that transgress their own deeply held moral code*, and the transgression cannot be metabolized or integrated.

The classic moral injury profile includes: persistent shame and guilt; loss of trust in self and institutions; spiritual/existential crisis; a tendency to either *collapse* (depressive withdrawal, sometimes suicide) or *escalate* (commit further transgressions, because to stop and feel the harm would shatter the self-image that justified the original transgression). Hank takes the second path, decisively.

The injuries, in order:

1. **Endangered Species (post-M-Day).** Consorts with Sinister, Dark Beast, High Evolutionary — geneticists he has spent his career opposing on principle — and *still fails to save the species*. The transgression compounds with the failure: he sold ethics, got nothing.
2. **The time-displacement of the original five.** Reckless action against unanimous objection, with cascading multi-year harm to the displaced teens.
3. **The Krakoan X-Force operations.** Assassination, the Terra Verde coup, the abuse of Colossus, the systematic use of resurrection as torture. Each act is by his own pre-Krakoan standards monstrous; each is committed under elaborate utilitarian justification.

The diagnostic tell of moral injury rather than ordinary guilt or remorse: *the subject does not stop, apologize, or restitute.* He continues, with each new transgression slightly larger, the justifying framework slightly more elaborate, the dissociation from his pre-injury self slightly more complete. By the time his peers execute him, the gap between the man speaking and the man he was at the Jean Grey School lectern is unbridgeable, and he himself does not seem to feel it as a gap. That is moral injury in late stage.

### 2.4 Body-Dysmorphic Undertow (subclinical, persistent, etiologically central)

He does not meet criteria for **Body Dysmorphic Disorder**. He does not avoid mirrors, conceal the perceived defect, seek corrective procedures, or experience the obsessional ruminations that disorder requires. He accepts each new form of his body, behaviorally.

But the *verbal* record over six decades is unambiguous: he cannot leave his appearance alone. Every conversation eventually contains a reference, usually self-mocking, occasionally self-savaging, to the fur, the feet, the fangs, the silhouette. He has a stock repertoire of self-descriptors (the "bouncing blue beast" register) that he deploys with a frequency a healthy adjustment would not require. This is best characterized as a **subclinical dysmorphic preoccupation**, ego-syntonic, managed by humor (a mature defense) but never resolved.

The etiology is direct: a visibly mutant child in a society that gawks at visible mutation does not get to develop a neutral relationship to his own body. He developed a *managed* one. The management is continuous and lifelong. It is not pathology in the disorder sense; it is the residue of a developmental wound that the OCP scaffolding partially but not completely covered.

### 2.5 Recurrent Situational Depressive Episodes (dysthymic undertow, not MDD)

The record shows multiple stretches of low mood, social withdrawal, increased work absorption, and what reads as anhedonia outside the lab. Each is reactive to identifiable stressors:

- The Trish Tilby breakup (her recoil from the secondary mutation).
- The post-Jean Grey deaths (multiple).
- The aftermath of M-Day.
- The post-Schism estrangement from Cyclops, a friendship that had defined four decades.
- The terminal diagnosis period.

In each, the episode is *time-limited*, *resolves into work*, and does not produce the neurovegetative cluster that **Major Depressive Disorder** requires — no documented major weight change attributable to mood (his eating is metabolic), no documented sleep collapse (he is a chronic short-sleeper at baseline), no suicidality, no psychomotor change of clinical magnitude, no persistent loss of interest across all domains.

The most accurate frame is **adjustment disorder with depressed mood, recurrent**, on a background of mild persistent depressive undertow (**dysthymia / persistent depressive disorder, subthreshold**). The dysthymic undertow is the affective baseline that the OCP work-immersion successfully masks for most of his life. It surfaces only when the work itself becomes the source of distress.

---

## 3. Symptom Presentation in Behavior (the granular map)

Translating the formulation into the specific behavioral signatures a surveillance dossier should index:

- **Speech register elevation under affective load.** When Hank is hurting, his vocabulary climbs. The presence of Latin tags, literary citations, and arch syntactic inversion in a given transcript is a reliable proxy for distress. The diagnostic inversion: when Hank speaks *plainly*, he is either at rest or past the point of defense — and the latter is rare and dangerous.
- **Marathon lab cycles as affect regulator.** Onset of a 24-hour-plus lab session within 48 hours of a significant loss or conflict is the most predictable single behavior in his record.
- **Self-reference in clinical third person.** "The patient appears to require…" "One observes that the subject…" Increases under bodily anxiety. A signature of isolation of affect.
- **Selective consultation pattern.** Across his career, who he calls when he is in trouble is a better indicator of his current ethical state than what he says. Pre-Decimation: Xavier, Jean, Reed Richards. Post-Decimation: villainous geneticists. Krakoa: nobody on the Quiet Council, no peer review at all. The consultation graph is the moral-injury chart.
- **Grooming jokes as anxiety indicator.** Frequency of fur/appearance self-deprecation in a given week scales with body-image stress, secondary-mutation drift, partner difficulty.
- **Cited authorities as ideology weather-vane.** When he is well, he quotes Shakespeare, Wilde, Twain, Byron — humanists. When he is bending, he quotes utilitarians and consequentialists. When he is in late-Krakoa mode, the citations thin to operational language: cost-benefit, asset, acceptable loss. The citation register is a real-time readout of where his ethics are.
- **Tactile fidgeting on his own forearm fur.** Self-soothing behavior, increases under stress, almost certainly unconscious.
- **Tea preparation as ritual.** The deliberate, slow tea ceremony he performs in his lab is best understood as the closest he comes to a *meditative* practice — and the only consistent break in his work-immersion pattern. Its absence in late-period Krakoa scenes is itself a datum.

---

## 4. Course Over Time

**Phase 1 (childhood–adolescence, Dunfee through Xavier recruitment).** OCP scaffolding builds. Dysmorphic undertow established. Compensatory dual-track (athletics + intellect) functioning. No syndromal pathology. Subject is *thriving* by external metric, *managing* by internal one.

**Phase 2 (original X-Men, late teens–early twenties).** Stable OCP, ego-syntonic. Humor and intellectualization mature defenses functioning. Romantic life functional. No clinical concern.

**Phase 3 (Brand Corporation, first self-transformation).** First major *iatrogenic* event — self-induced. Acute presentation of confusion and altered behavior; resolves. The diagnostic note: the *willingness* to self-experiment is the OCP-perfectionist refusal to expose others to risk *and* the early form of the unilateralism that will later metastasize.

**Phase 4 (Avengers period).** Best-adjusted stretch of the file. The high society environment grants the *useful intellectual* identity room to flourish without the *hunted mutant* overlay. Romantic life active. Friendship with Wonder Man stable and reciprocal. OCP visible but compensated. No comorbidities active.

**Phase 5 (X-Factor through 90s X-Men).** Re-immersion in mutant-as-quarry stress. OCP intensifies. Sublimation into science vocation deepens. Trish Tilby relationship and its end produces first major adult depressive episode, well-managed. Conscience-role on the team consolidates — and with it the seed of the over-investment in his own moral judgment that becomes lethal later.

**Phase 6 (Morrison era, secondary mutation, public sexuality provocation).** Body-anxiety surge. Reaction-formation aesthetic ramps. Self-staging as rhetorical instrument debuts at scale. Still functional. The OCP rigidity acquires a *performative* dimension — he is no longer just doing the work, he is *publicly being the kind of person who does this work*. This is the prodromal phase of the narcissistic overlay, retrospectively.

**Phase 7 (Decimation / Endangered Species).** First major moral injury. He compromises with monsters and fails. The defensive structure cannot metabolize the failure; it converts the residue into intensified resolve rather than acknowledged shame. Beginning of the slide.

**Phase 8 (Schism, Jean Grey School, terminal diagnosis, time-travel decision).** Acute narcissistic decompensation. The terminal frame removes the long-time-horizon brake on unilateral action. Time-travel decision is the threshold-crossing event after which the structure is qualitatively different.

**Phase 9 (Krakoa, X-Force, the assassinations).** Late-stage syndrome fully expressed. OCP perfectionism + acquired narcissism + accumulated moral injury produce a functioning spymaster whose internal ethical brake is broken in the specific sense described: he can still *generate* ethical reasoning, exuberantly, but the reasoning no longer *constrains* the action; it *follows* the action and *justifies* it.

**Phase 10 (execution by peers, replacement by earlier-resurrection Hank).** The system around him discharges him, in the most literal possible sense. Diagnostically, this is the *external* recognition that internal correction had become impossible.

**Predictive note.** If the earlier-resurrection Hank persists in the same role with the same stressors, the same trajectory will recur on a compressed timeline. The personality structure is the same; only the moral-injury ledger has been zeroed. Without changes to the role demands and to the absence of meaningful peer oversight, decompensation Phase 7 onward is the *expected* outcome, not a contingent one.

---

## 5. Comorbidity Map

- **OCP × acquired narcissism.** Synergistic. The perfectionism feeds the special-person belief; the special-person belief licenses the perfectionist's intolerance of others' input.
- **OCP × moral injury.** Particularly destructive. OCP individuals have unusually rigid ethical codes; when they transgress them, they cannot do the cognitive flexibility work that allows non-OCP individuals to grieve, atone, and reintegrate. They instead *re-justify*, which the OCP intellectual machinery is uniquely well-equipped to do.
- **Acquired narcissism × moral injury.** The narcissistic decompensation prevents the shame from doing its proper function (course correction); the moral injury escalates because the shame has no metabolic outlet.
- **Dysmorphic undertow × intellectualization.** Mutually reinforcing. The body anxiety is managed by the cognitive performance; the cognitive performance is *for* the body anxiety; neither can be modified without addressing the other.

No comorbid substance use disorder. No comorbid anxiety disorder meeting criteria. No comorbid psychotic disorder. No comorbid eating disorder (his hyperphagia is metabolic). No comorbid PTSD meeting criteria (see Differential below).

---

## 6. Differential Diagnosis — What He Is *Not*, and Why

A long list, because most of the casual readings of this subject get this wrong.

### Not Antisocial Personality / Sociopathy

The Krakoan record tempts this reading and the temptation must be refused. Antisocial individuals do not require justification; they do not generate moral frameworks for their transgressions; they do not experience the persistent shame and guilt that the moral injury frame requires. Hank generates baroque ethical justifications precisely *because* his conscience is present and functioning — broken, but present. A sociopath would not need the prose. The prose is the diagnostic evidence against the diagnosis.

Additional disqualifiers: childhood conduct disorder absent; capacity for loyalty across decades demonstrated; remorse signals visible (the deepening bitterness in his humor; the increasing avoidance of his pre-Krakoa friends; the documented late-period insomnia not present in earlier files).

### Not Bipolar / Manic-Spectrum

His marathon work cycles, grand projects, and elaborated verbal output superficially mimic hypomania. They are not. They are *trait baseline*, not *episodic*. There is no documented periodicity. There are no depressive poles meeting MDE criteria. There is no documented decreased need for sleep arising acutely against a baseline of normal sleep (he has *always* been a short-sleeper). There is no flight of ideas in the technical sense — his associative speech is *organized* and *productive*, not loose. There are no documented manic-spectrum decisional patterns of the impulsive financial / sexual / risk-taking type. The time-travel decision is grandiose but it is *planned*, *premeditated*, *justified in advance* — exactly the wrong cognitive shape for mania.

### Not Schizoid / Schizotypal

He is gregarious, romantically active across decades, friend-dense, capable of intimacy. He has no magical thinking, no ideas of reference, no perceptual aberrations, no oddities of speech in the schizotypal sense (his eccentricity is *cultivated*, not *intrinsic*). Rule out cleanly.

### Not Paranoid

Even at his most operationally suspicious, on Krakoa, his model of threats is *accurate to the world he inhabits* (the world genuinely contains anti-mutant conspiracies). His error is in *solutions*, not *threat perception*. He does not over-attribute hostile intent; he over-attributes *his own capacity* to act unilaterally. This is narcissistic-grandiose error, not paranoid error.

### Not Obsessive-Compulsive Disorder (the anxiety disorder)

No intrusive ego-dystonic thoughts. No neutralizing rituals. No checking, counting, contamination, or symmetry compulsions. The conflation with OCP must be refused; they are different entities. His scrupulousness is moral and


## Behavioral Atlas

# BEHAVIORAL ATLAS: HENRY PHILIP McCOY

*Compiled from longitudinal observation across the published record, 1963–present. Read as a field manual: what the subject does, in what order, with what body, under each named condition. Distinguishes baseline from departure, conscious display from involuntary tell, early-period habit from late-period drift.*

---

## I. BASELINE — THE CALM, AT-HOME McCOY

The unstressed McCoy is the man most observers think of as "the real one." This is misleading. The calm presentation is itself a curated performance, rehearsed over fifty years, and its components are diagnostic.

**Posture and locomotion.** Default standing posture is an unconscious *plié*: knees slightly flexed, weight rolled forward onto the balls of the (oversized) feet, heels rarely planted. He does not stand still the way humans stand still; he *idles*, like a quadruped at rest, occasionally shifting weight side to side. When seated, he gravitates to surfaces that allow squatting or perching — counters, lab stools, the backs of couches, windowsills, chair-arms instead of cushions. A proper sit, knees-down in an armchair, is reserved for performances of normality (parlor, faculty meeting, dinner with civilians). The perching is involuntary; the sitting is theater.

**Hands.** Constant low-grade fidget. Pen-spinning, paperclip-bending, the rolling of a chess piece across the knuckles, the unconscious flexing-and-splaying of fingers as if testing their range. He brings hands to his face frequently — knuckle to chin, finger to lip, the back of the hand to the bridge of the nose. Late-period (post-secondary mutation) he grooms: a single swipe of forefinger and thumb down a sideburn, a smoothing of the mane behind one ear. The grooming gesture is new equipment; the hand-to-face is forty years old.

**Eyes.** Tracks rapidly across a room on entry — windows, exits, persons, available improvised weapons, the nearest elevated surface. This is so habitual it does not register on his face. He locks eye contact warmly in dyads, breaks it upward (not down) when thinking — eyes to ceiling or middle distance over the interlocutor's shoulder. The upward break is the *intellectualization tell*: he is about to reach for a phrase.

**Voice.** Resting register is a warm baritone, slightly slower than American conversational baseline, with the consonantal precision of someone who learned diction from books rather than peers.
