**GIVEN** the chance to be the one who saves *everyone*:
**EXPECT** him to take it, every time. The savior posture is not a flaw he can see; it is the structural shape of his self-respect. Anyone offering him a sufficiently large stage will get a yes.

---

## 8. THE WOUND — SPECIFIC TOUCHES

These predictions are keyed to the precise contact points of the childhood injury.

**GIVEN** he is described publicly as an *animal, beast, freak, monster, thing* — not in friendly self-deprecation but with intent:
**EXPECT** a smile, a slight tilt of the head, a witticism that lands like a knife in silk, and a private cost that will surface days later as snappishness with subordinates or a missed appointment. The wound bypasses the in-room defenses and exits through indirect channels.

**GIVEN** he is photographed or filmed in a context that emphasizes his physicality over his speech (eating, grooming, in motion at full feral extension):
**EXPECT** subsequent overcorrection in the next public appearance — formalwear, a prepared remark, a poem. The compensatory rhythm is reliable enough to be choreographed against.

**GIVEN** a child looks at him with fear:
**EXPECT** a softening that overrides any tactical posture he is holding. He will lower himself physically (sit, crouch, drop to one knee), gentle his voice into a register he uses with no one else, and produce — almost involuntarily — some small bit of patter or sleight of hand. This is the seventeen-year-old still trying to prove he is not what he looks like. It is unguarded and exploitable. Confidence: very high.

**GIVEN** he is out-thought in front of his peers — not in friendly contest but in a way that publicly establishes another mind as senior to his on his own ground:
**EXPECT** a graceful concession in the moment ("touché, that is well-reasoned") and a multi-week project initiated in private to demonstrate, on adjacent ground, that the concession was situational rather than structural. He cannot leave the ranking unrestored. The behavior is invisible in the room and visible in the calendar.

**GIVEN** he is in a romantic context where the partner sees the fur and falters:
**EXPECT** him to register the falter inside half a second, to cover for the partner verbally and gallantly, and to remove himself from the situation within the hour under an excuse that flatters the partner. The wound here is not anger; it is *recognition of an old verdict being confirmed again*, and the response is to spare the partner the work of withdrawing.

**GIVEN** he is in the presence of a person who knew him before the first transformation (an aging former classmate, a parent's old friend, a teammate from the first cohort):
**EXPECT** a quality of attention to that person disproportionate to their current relevance. They are evidence; he honors them. He will remember absurd small details from decades prior and produce them as a gift.

**GIVEN** anniversaries of his transformations (the Brand Corporation date, the secondary mutation event):
**EXPECT** subtle behavior shifts in the surrounding week — a return to a particular composer, a longer solo session in the lab, a deflection of social plans. He does not name these anniversaries. They are observable only in the negative space of the calendar.

---

## 9. DECOMPENSATION-EDGE — THE FOUR-STAGE PROFILE, INSTRUMENTED

Restating the stress-escalation profile in predictive form, with observable markers a watcher could log.

**STAGE 1 — Verbal Densification.** Sentences lengthen. Latin and Greek tags rise from baseline frequency. Literary citation broadens from his usual nineteenth-century English canon into earlier and more obscure sources (Lucretius, the metaphysical poets). Humor remains warm but becomes more elaborate. **Observable marker:** average sentence length in unprompted speech doubles. **Intervention window:** wide. He can still be reached by a direct personal appeal from a trusted intimate at this stage.

**STAGE 2 — Lab Retreat.** Sleep contracts; lab hours extend. Social obligations begin to be declined with elaborately courteous regret. Teaching gets covered. Phone and mail backlog grows; he claims to be answering it; he is not. **Observable marker:** unanswered correspondence from his closest circle (the test is *not* whether strangers' messages go unanswered — those always do — but whether Bobby's do). **Intervention window:** narrowing. He can still be reached, but it now requires physical presence; remote contact bounces off.

**STAGE 3 — Unilateral Planning.** The justificatory prose begins assembling in his head and surfaces in fragments to chosen confidants. He stops asking opinions and begins *presenting* arguments. Body language shifts subtly toward presentation posture even in private — shoulders squarer, hands more often clasped behind his back, a slight rhetorical lift to declarative sentences. **Observable marker:** he stops asking questions in team meetings and begins making statements. **Intervention window:** narrow. Only a peer he respects as an ethical equal can interrupt the trajectory here, and even then only by refusing to engage with the prose on its own terms.

**STAGE 4 — Instrumentation of Others.** The threshold is crossed when he proposes, or undertakes, a plan that uses allies or innocents as means without their informed consent. By the time this stage is visible, the prior stages have completed and the rationalization engine is at full power. **Observable marker:** the appearance, in his speech, of phrases like *what is required of us* and *the cost we must accept* — first-person plural carrying weight that should be carried by individuals. **Intervention window:** effectively closed by ordinary means. At this stage the historical record indicates that *only catastrophic external consequence, or coercive removal by his peers, has reliably arrested him.* This is the verdict the Krakoan endgame delivered, and it should be read as data, not melodrama.

---

## 10. SUMMARY MATRIX — TOP-LINE LEVERS

For analysts operating in real-time, the following are the highest-confidence single-input predictors of his behavior:

- **To predict whether he will act unilaterally:** check for terminal-framing of the situation (his own mortality, species mortality, or any frame that removes personal-cost from his calculus). Presence of such framing is the strongest single predictor.
- **To predict whether he will accept a corrupting offer:** check whether the offer flatters his *unique ethical-technical capability* rather than his power or wealth. The former is decisive; the latter inert.
- **To predict whether he can be talked out of a decision:** check the stage. Stages 1–2, yes, by intimates. Stage 3, only by ethical peers. Stage 4, no.
- **To predict where he is most exploitable:** academic recognition, the savior stage, and any framing that makes refusal look like cowardice in front of the original five.
- **To predict where he is most protectable:** in the presence of students, of children showing fear, of Bobby Drake, and in the bounded technical crisis. These contexts reliably summon the early self.
- **To predict the shape of his eventual fall, should it come again:** it will not look like collapse. It will look like a meticulously reasoned argument, delivered in his best voice, justifying an act his younger self would have refused. The fall is always articulate. The articulacy is the symptom.

*— End Section.*


## Vulnerabilities & Leverage Compendium

# VULNERABILITIES & LEVERAGE COMPENDIUM: HENRY PHILIP McCOY

*Pressure-point cartography. Oriented toward understanding, protection, and — where the subject's own trajectory requires it — informed intervention by those who love him. Every lever named here can be pulled by an adversary; the purpose of naming them is to allow allies to monitor, pre-empt, and harden them first.*

---

## 1. PRELIMINARIES: HOW HE PROCESSES THREAT AT ALL

Before listing levers, the operator must understand the *transduction layer* between any stimulus and Hank's behavior. Stimuli do not reach his affect directly; they are routed through three serial filters.

1. **The lexical filter.** A stressor first triggers verbal output — a quip, a citation, an arch reframing. If you cannot get him *past* this filter, you have not actually reached him. He can converse fluently for hours from inside it while registering nothing below.
2. **The competence filter.** Whatever survives the lexical filter is then re-evaluated as a *problem*. He converts emotional or interpersonal stress into a soluble engineering question. If he can name an experiment, a calculation, or a procedure that addresses it, the affect drops out and the work absorbs it.
3. **The moral-mathematics filter.** Whatever survives *that* is loaded into his ethical calculator and resolved into a course of action he then defends in airtight prose.

The vulnerabilities below are organized by which filter they bypass, exploit, or jam. The most dangerous levers — the ones that destabilize him, for good or ill — are those that reach beneath all three.

---

## 2. THE BODY: THE FOUNDATIONAL LEVER

Every other vulnerability sits downstream of this one. The visible mutation from birth is the original wound; sixty years of armor have not closed it.

**To reach him through the body.** The single most reliable way to register *with* Hank is to treat the fur, claws, fangs, and feline carriage as utterly unremarkable — to look him in the eye for a full beat longer than strangers do, to shake the oversized hand without flinching, to hand him a teacup made for human fingers without commenting on the mismatch. Trish Tilby in her early period, Wonder Man across decades, and Bobby Drake from the first day do this instinctively. He registers it. He marks the person, durably, as *safe terrain*.

**To calm him through the body.** Physical companionship without remark. Sitting in the same lab. Sharing food (he is an enormous eater; provisioning him *without ceremony* lands harder than verbal reassurance). Allowing him to groom in your presence — the obsessive smoothing of fur on the forearm, the running of clawed fingers through the mane — without watching it as a curiosity.

**To wound him through the body.** This is the most accessible attack surface and the one adversaries reach for first.
- *Diminutives applied to his form.* "Pet." "Kitty." "Fido." "The animal." A trained operator who deploys these in front of an audience he respects will produce stage-1 escalation (heightened verbal performance) within thirty seconds.
- *Comparative framing.* Standing him next to a baseline human and inviting comparison — height differential, glove sizes, doorways too short. The Brotherhood and Mystique have used variants of this.
- *Mirrors, unexpectedly.* He has adapted to mirrors he chose to install; an *uninvited* full-length reflection — a window, a polished surface, a holo display — momentarily catches him. Look for a half-second silence, the only such silence he produces.
- *Reminding him what he used to look like.* Photographs from the pre-*Amazing Adventures #11* period. Cerebro projections of the original-five teen body. Time-displaced young Hank himself, in the room with him, is the maximal form of this attack — and the canon shows he could not metabolize it.
- *Romantic abandonment citing the body as cause.* The Tilby pattern. Any partner who leaves and lets the reason be visibly somatic re-opens the original wound at full depth.

**To predict him through the body.** When his somatic self-references *increase* in density in a conversation, he is under stress he has not yet named. When they *cease entirely*, he has progressed past stage 2 into the work cycle and is no longer accessible by ordinary means.

---

## 3. INTELLECT AS BOTH MOAT AND BREACH

His mind is his proudest asset and his most exploitable one. The same surface protects him from most attempts to reach him and exposes him to a narrow class of attempts that don't.

**To reach him intellectually.** Bring him a real problem he has not seen. Not flattery — flattery insults him because he detects it instantly. A *genuine* unsolved technical or ethical knot, presented with the honest admission that you cannot resolve it, opens a door no emotional appeal will. His vocation is *being asked the question no one else can answer*; honor that vocation and you have his attention indefinitely.

**To calm him intellectually.** Slow the dialogue down. Ask him to *explain*, to *teach*, to *narrate the derivation*. Teaching is his settled state — Jean Grey School Hank is observably the most regulated Hank in the record. Putting him in the pedagogical posture downshifts him through all three filters into something like rest.

**To persuade him intellectually.** Three rules.
1. *Never argue from authority.* He outranks almost any authority you can cite, and treating consensus as decisive triggers his contempt.
2. *Argue from his own prior statements.* He keeps faith with his earlier ethical formulations more than with any external code. Quoting Hank-at-twenty-five to Hank-at-sixty is the single highest-yield rhetorical move available.
3. *Give him the dignity of changing his mind privately.* Public reversal is humiliation; he will dig in. A conversation in his lab, no witnesses, no recording, with an exit graceful enough to look like *his* idea, will move him when a faculty meeting will not.

**To provoke him intellectually.** Suggest he has been out-thought by a specific named peer — Sinister, Reed Richards, Doom, even Forge in his domain. This produces stage 2 (lab withdrawal, marathon cycles) reliably. Suggest he has been out-thought by *Cyclops*, late period, and it produces stage 3.

**To destabilize him intellectually.** This is the dangerous one and the only attack vector that has consistently worked against him across canon. *Reframe his moral certainty as motivated reasoning, with receipts, in front of someone whose opinion he values.* The accusation alone he can metabolize — he has a paragraph ready. The accusation *with citation*, *delivered by a witness he cannot dismiss*, with the *receipts laid on the table in his own handwriting*, jams all three filters at once. The lexical filter cannot quip past his own annotations. The competence filter cannot reframe the problem because he authored the problem. The moral filter cannot generate justification because the justification is what's on trial. This is the only known method to reliably produce, in Hank, the silence that means actual reception.

It is also the method that, applied without love, breaks him.

---

## 4. THE INNER CIRCLE: LOVE AS LEVER

He loves a small number of people very durably. The list, across canon: Robert Drake; Jean Grey; Warren Worthington; Scott Summers (estranged but never erased); Wonder Man; Vera Cantor and then Trish Tilby in their respective eras; Abigail Brand; Charles Xavier (complicated); his parents Norton and Edna. These are the people through whom he can be reached at depths his own defenses cannot guard.

**Bobby Drake** is the master key. The friendship is the longest continuous relationship in his adult life and the one in which he is least performative. Bobby can say things to him no one else can say. An ally who needs Hank to *hear* something difficult should, if possible, route it through Bobby. An adversary who wants to wound Hank should target Bobby — and Hank's record of overreaction when Bobby is endangered is a vulnerability he has never patched.

**Jean Grey** is the unhealed grief. Her deaths and resurrections are the only events that have produced visible affective dysregulation in him — pauses, voice-cracks, abandoned sentences. The presence of Jean, in any incarnation, downshifts him; her absence raises his baseline anxiety in ways he will not name.

**Wonder Man** is the *non-mutant* friend, the one relationship that proves to him he can be loved outside the conditions of mutant solidarity. Simon Williams's regard is structurally irreplaceable; any threat to that friendship cuts deeper than threats internal to the X-community.

**Trish Tilby** remains the unhealed romantic wound. Mentioning her, even in passing, produces a measurable shift — a half-second's lexical pause, a slightly tighter verbal performance for the rest of the conversation. He has never written a clean ending for her in his own internal narrative.

**The original five as a unit** are the only people on Earth who *knew him before the fur*. They are the witnesses to the self the body keeps erasing. Threats to them register as threats to his continuity-of-self, not merely to teammates. Conversely, when all five are in the same room, Hank is calibrated, calmer, more honest, more accessible than in any other configuration.

**To protect him, monitor these relationships actively.** When Hank withdraws from Bobby, when he stops speaking of Jean, when he ceases his standing correspondence with Simon Williams — these are leading indicators of stage 3 escalation, often weeks before unilateral action.

---

## 5. SHAME, GUILT, AND THE MORAL-INJURY SURFACE

Guilt is the affective system that did *not* get successfully isolated. It still gets through. This is the channel through which he can be reached when intellect cannot reach him, and the channel through which, if overloaded, he can be destroyed.

**To reach him through guilt.** Specificity. Not "you have hurt people" — he has an essay ready. *Name the person, name the harm, name the date, name what they said the next morning.* Colossus's words after a resurrection. The face of one of the time-displaced teens in their first week in the present. The names of those who died in Terra Verde. He cannot deflect a name and a date with a Latin tag.

**To calm him through guilt.** Counterintuitively: *forgiveness from an unimpeachable source*. Not exoneration, which insults him, but a serious, eyes-open, costed acknowledgment from someone who has earned the standing — Bobby; Storm; a Jean — that the harm is real and the person speaking will nevertheless remain in relation. This is the only intervention known to *halt* his rationalization engine mid-spiral rather than merely interrupt it.

**To destabilize him through guilt.** Force him into the room with someone he has wronged who is not interested in his explanation. The canonical scene — his teammates having him killed and replaced — is the maximal version. Lesser versions: arrange a sustained working partnership with someone whose injury at his hands he cannot rhetorically dissolve, and who is not cruel enough to confront him about it but not gracious enough to pretend it didn't happen. The ambient unresolved obligation will eat at him in a way confrontation will not.

**Warning.** Guilt overload is the failure mode that produced the late-period escalations in the first place. The moral-injury loop runs: *transgression → unbearable guilt → cannot bear it → must justify it → must commit further transgression to validate the justification.* An operator wishing to *protect* Hank from himself must dose guilt carefully, with relational scaffolding present, never as raw exposure.

---

## 6. MORTALITY AND UNFINISHED BUSINESS

The terminal-diagnosis behavior is the most important data point in the entire file. When Hank believes he is dying *with the species-problem unsolved*, he becomes capable of decisions he would otherwise have rejected. The time-travel decision is the canonical example.

**Implication for monitoring.** Any medical event suggesting limited remaining time is a red-flag stimulus, regardless of the actual prognosis. Resolution of the medical issue does not fully reset behavior; the *experience* of having decided under terminal framing leaves a residue of permissive precedent.

**To calm him under mortality pressure.** Provide credible succession. Show him the apprentices, the published papers, the institutional structures that will continue the work without him. The Jean Grey School functions partly as a calming mechanism in exactly this register. *Being replaceable in the work* is paradoxically what permits him to die unhurriedly; *believing himself irreplaceable* is what produces the catastrophic decisions.

**To provoke him under mortality pressure.** Suggest the work will die with him. Suggest no one else can finish it. Any framing of unique indispensability, combined with limited time, will produce a unilateral action of escalating consequence.

---

## 7. AUTHORITY, CONSENSUS, AND THE DELIBERATIVE BRAKE

Hank's relationship to group decision is the single weakest point in his operational architecture.

**The pattern.** He participates in deliberation up to the moment he concludes the deliberation is wrong, at which point he ceases to participate in any meaningful sense while *continuing to attend the meetings*. The performance of collegiality persists; the substance has been withdrawn. By the time peers notice, he has already begun acting on the conclusion he reached privately.

**To detect the withdrawal early.** Look for the shift from *advocacy* to *summary*. Hank-in-deliberation argues; Hank-who-has-decided neutrally restates the positions in the room with apparent fairness, declines to advance his own further, and offers a concluding witticism that gracefully changes the subject. The witticism-as-exit is the tell. Once observed, assume the unilateral track is already in motion and act on a compressed timeline.

**To re-engage him into consensus.** Confront the withdrawal directly, privately, with an offer he cannot refuse: a *real* role in the decision rather than a vote whose outcome he predicts. He will not return to a process he believes is theater. He will return to one in which his specific competencies are necessary to the outcome. Xavier knew this. Storm knows this. Cyclops, late period, forgot it, and the cost was steep.

**To provoke unilateral action.** Trivially easy. Convene a body, exclude him, decide a matter in his domain, present him with the decision as fait accompli. The probability of an unsanctioned countermove approaches unity.

---

## 8. THE PROFESSIONAL SURFACES — WHAT TO SAY AND NOT SAY

A short field manual for those who must interact with him under various postures.

**To open warmly.** A specific reference to a recent paper, a teaching moment, or a piece of music he is known to favor. Not the body. Not the team. Something *individuated to his mind and taste*. He will respond at length and the conversation will be productive.

**To open under stress.** Acknowledge the stressor by name, briefly, without rhetoric, then offer a concrete next step. He will accept brevity from a peer where he will not accept either evasion or extended emotional engagement.

**To deliver bad news.** Privately, in his lab or his quarters, with the data on the table, with time allowed for him to read it himself before you speak. He must be permitted to process technically before he is asked to respond personally. Violating this sequence — emotional address first, data second — produces the lexical filter at full deflection and the conversation is wasted.

**To deliver praise.** Sparingly, specifically, and never in the register of "you are extraordinary." He distrusts that register on principle. Praise the work product; let him infer the rest.

**To deliver criticism.** Quote him to himself. Cite a prior Hank against the present one. Frame the criticism as continuity-of-self rather than external judgment. Anything else triggers defenses he has had decades to refine.

**To request a favor.** Make it a hard problem. Easy favors he resents as beneath him; hard problems he accepts as tribute.

**To refuse him.** Refuse on technical grounds, not moral ones. A "no" framed in terms of feasibility he will accept and work around; a "no" framed in terms of ethics he will read as a challenge to his own ethical reasoning and may escalate against.

---

## 9. ENVIRONMENTAL AND ROUTINE LEVERS

Habits and routes through which he can be reached, monitored, or — by an adversary — predicted.

**The lab as both sanctuary and tell.** Lab presence is his settled state. *Absence from the lab during a known crisis* means he is in the field, almost certainly without authorization. *Excessive presence in the lab — more than forty-eight hours continuous — means he is in stage 2 escalation and an intervention should be staged before stage 3 lands.* Bring food, sit down, do not ask what he is working on; ask what he is *avoiding*.

**Sleep deprivation as accelerant.** Hank's defenses degrade measurably with sleep loss, but not in the directions one might expect — his speech becomes *more* baroque, his humor *darker*, his ethical reasoning *faster and less audited*. A Hank who has not slept in three days is the Hank most likely to make a stage-3 decision. Sleep monitoring is, unglamorously, one of the highest-yield protective interventions available to those around him.

**The wardrobe as register.** He dresses with care. The dressing gown, the velvet jacket, the cravats, the half-moon spectacles he does not need — these are the *peace* uniform, signaling regulated state. A Hank in lab whites for days at a stretch, or in field gear past mission necessity, has departed the peace state. The cultural costuming is reaction-formation in fabric form; its absence is a warning.

**Music as ambient signal.** Opera in the lab: working calmly. Bach: working hard. Silence with the door closed: do not enter without escalation authority.

**The standing correspondences.** Hank maintains active written or comm relationships with a small number of correspondents on long cycles. Lapses in these correspondences — Bobby letters going unanswered, the standing call with Wonder Man missed — are reliable leading indicators of withdrawal, often weeks ahead of behavioral evidence.

**Food.** He eats enormously and ritually. Skipped meals are diagnostic. A Hank who declines breakfast is not himself; a Hank who declines two consecutive meals requires medical eyes on him.

---

## 10. ADVERSARIAL VECTORS — WHAT OPPONENTS WILL ACTUALLY USE

The threat-model exercise. An informed adversary, having studied this file, would pursue Hank along the following axes, in approximately this order of yield.

1. *Manufactured terminal framing.* A false or accelerated medical diagnosis, or the credible appearance of one. Combined with isolation, this is the most reliable known method to elicit catastrophic unilateral action from him.
2. *A genuinely interesting problem with hidden cost.* A puzzle worthy of him whose solution requires moral compromise he can rationalize. Sinister's longstanding playbook. He has accepted this bait before and will again.
3. *Targeting the inner circle.* Direct threat to Bobby, to Jean in whatever form she takes, to Wonder Man, to the original five collectively. His response will be overwhelming, predictable, and exploitable.
4. *Public somatic humiliation paired with intellectual challenge.* Forces him to defend two flanks at once; defenses degrade visibly.
5. *Cultivating his certainty.* The subtlest attack. Agree with his moral reasoning; supply additional rationale; flatter the calculus. He is more vulnerable to allies than to enemies, because allies bypass the contempt filter.
6. *Removal from deliberative bodies.* Drive him to act alone by ensuring he has no legitimate channel; then point to the unilateral action as evidence of unfitness. The Krakoa-era dynamic, in part.

The defensive corollary: those who love him should *anticipate these vectors and harden against them in advance*, particularly (1), (3), and (5), which are the least visible to him.

---

## 11. THE PROTECTIVE READ — WHAT KEEPS HIM WELL

The compendium concludes where it must: with the conditions under which Hank McCoy is *good, regulated, and accessible to himself*. These are the conditions an ally maintains.

- *A real problem worth his mind, with a deadline that is challenging but not terminal.*
- *A small number of people who knew him before — and after — and have not flinched.*
- *Students. Specifically students who are not yet his equals and will not be for years. The pedagogical posture downshifts him reliably.*
- *Adequate sleep, adequate food, and the wardrobe that signals peace.*
- *A deliberative body whose process he respects and whose authority over him he accepts. The lack of this in late canon is not incidental to his fall; it is causal.*
- *At least one person empowered and trusted to say "Hank, you are wrong, and here is the paragraph from you in 1985 that proves it" — and to be heard.*
- *Forgiveness, costed and credible, from someone who has earned the standing to grant it, when guilt accumulates faster than he can metabolize it.*
- *Acknowledgment, periodically, that he is loved for reasons that have nothing to do with his usefulness.* The last is the one his own defensive architecture cannot supply him. It must be brought from outside, and brought repeatedly, because the architecture will keep trying to discount it.

The file's bleakest finding and its most hopeful one are the same finding: *Hank McCoy can be reached.* By the right hands, with the right tools, at the right time, the man under the armor is still there — the seventeen-year-old quoting Byron not to deflect but to share something he found beautiful. Everything in this compendium that can be used to harm him can be used, with care, to bring him home.


## Strengths, Assets & Resilience

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 6: STRENGTHS, ASSETS & RESILIENCE

*Subject: McCoy, Henry Philip. The positive ledger. What he is, what he has, what holds, and why.*

---

## 6.1 COGNITIVE ASSETS

### 6.1.1 The Apex Intellect (substantive, not honorific)

The first and largest entry on this ledger is the mind itself, and the file must be precise about its texture because "genius" as a label conceals more than it reveals. The subject is not a one-domain prodigy. He is a *polymathic synthesizer* whose working competence covers, at minimum: human and mutant genetics (PhD-equivalent, demonstrably operating at the frontier — he is among the small handful of geneticists on Earth Sinister and the High Evolutionary regard as peers); biochemistry; molecular and cellular biology; theoretical physics sufficient to engineer time-displacement apparatus from first principles; applied engineering across electronics, robotics, and aerospace (he maintains and modifies Blackbird-class aircraft, designs Cerebro upgrades, builds his own lab from scratch on multiple occasions); pharmacology; medicine and surgery at trauma-team level; and the humanities to a depth that is not ornament — he can argue a literary or ethical point on the merits, not merely garnish a sentence with a quotation.

The operational signature of this intellect is **cross-domain analogical reasoning at speed**. Watch him in any panel of working dialogue and the pattern is consistent: a biological problem is reframed via an engineering metaphor and solved with a tool borrowed from physics, while a literary citation supplies the ethical scaffold. This is not affectation. It is the actual cognitive process — he reasons by lateral leap, and the leaps land. It makes him irreplaceable on any team whose problems cross categories, which is virtually every problem the X-Men face.

### 6.1.2 Speed and Stamina of Cognition

He is a chronic short-sleeper who routinely sustains 30-hour lab cycles, and — critically — the *quality* of his fourth-shift output does not visibly degrade. He has a long working memory, a fast retrieval lattice, and the ability to hold multiple competing models simultaneously without collapsing one into the other prematurely. This last is the rarest skill in his cohort and explains why he is consistently the one to whom Xavier, Storm, and (until the schism) Cyclops bring problems that have already defeated everyone else.

### 6.1.3 Pedagogical Talent

A separate asset from raw intelligence and equally durable: he can *transmit* what he knows. The Jean Grey School period documents this in detail — students learn from him, retain what they learn, and remember him affectionately afterwards. He pitches register precisely to audience; he tolerates the slow student without contempt; he turns lab failures into teaching cases. The trait is structural, not seasonal — he was already explaining things to Bobby Drake in the original mansion era. A mind this gifted that is also a *teacher* is a force multiplier the institution depends on.

---

## 6.2 PHYSICAL ASSETS

### 6.2.1 The Combat Envelope

Pre-transformation, the body was already a tier above Olympic — strength, agility, and reflex speed in the 4–5x baseline range, with a center-of-gravity sense that produced his trademark acrobatic combat style. Post-mutagenic transformation and again post–secondary mutation, the envelope expanded: superhuman strength sufficient to engage Hulk-class opponents in restraint scenarios (not to defeat, but to delay), claws and fangs as fallback weapons, enhanced senses (smell, night vision, hearing), and a kinesthetic intelligence that lets him fight in three dimensions — walls, ceilings, the undersides of aircraft — in ways that disorient any opponent who has trained against bipedal templates.

The combat asset is not merely the body. It is the *body driven by the mind*. He is one of a very small number of fighters who diagnose opponents in real time — biomechanical weaknesses, breathing patterns, joint tolerances — and adjust mid-engagement. He doesn't out-power; he out-thinks at full physical speed.

### 6.2.2 Durability and Recovery

The catalogue of injuries he has metabolized and recovered from is, taken in aggregate, extraordinary: Sentinel maulings, neurotoxin exposures, Magneto-tier impacts, beatings from his Dark Beast counterpart, biological-weapon exposures during Legacy Virus research. Recovery is fast, complete, and — diagnostically — *unaccompanied by visible convalescent behavior*. He returns to work. This is partly enhanced physiology and partly a psychological refusal to occupy patient-status, but the operational result is the same: he is rarely off-line.

### 6.2.3 Self-Maintenance Competence

He is his own physician. He performs surgery on himself and on teammates routinely, manages his own metabolic and endocrine peculiarities (the increased caloric load, the altered thermoregulation), and has the rare hybrid skill of being able to *diagnose* his own body with a clinician's detachment. In a milieu where mutant physiology breaks standard medicine, this is a survival asset.

---

## 6.3 ETHICAL & MORAL ASSETS (THE EARLY-TO-MIDDLE LEDGER)

The collapse documented elsewhere in this file should not obscure the fact that for roughly forty of his sixty published years, the subject's ethical conduct was a load-bearing pillar of the X-Men institution. Specific durable strengths:

- **Conscience-first framing of technical questions.** He is the team member who reliably asks *should we* before *can we*. The Legacy Virus work, the early genetics research, the Cerebro-class projects — all bear his fingerprints precisely because Xavier knew that Hank would not let the engineering run ahead of the ethics. That this brake eventually failed under sustained moral injury does not retroactively erase the decades it held.
- **Whistleblower instinct.** In *Amazing Adventures* #11 and again in multiple Brand Corporation and government-contract storylines, he is the one who refuses to look away from institutional malfeasance and pays personal cost to expose it. The instinct is durable across eras.
- **Refusal to instrumentalize teammates (early-to-middle period).** Until the Krakoa-era inversion, he is conspicuously the team member who *will not* use allies as means. He volunteers himself as test subject precisely so no one else has to be.
- **Truthfulness with self about scientific limits.** Pre-Endangered Species, he is unusually willing to say *I do not know* and *this cannot be done*. This honesty is what kept him from earlier catastrophes.

---

## 6.4 RELATIONAL ASSETS

### 6.4.1 The Long-Bond Pattern

The single most underrated entry on his asset ledger is his capacity for *durable* friendship. Most figures in his cohort have intense, episodic, breakup-prone bonds; the subject has *forty-year* friendships. Robert Drake is a continuous bond from age sixteen to the present — that relationship has survived schisms, depowerings, deaths, resurrections, sexual-identity disclosures, and the subject's own moral collapse. Simon Williams is a similarly long, similarly resilient bond, weathering separation by team and by literal death. Jean Grey was a bond of comparable depth. These are not professional alliances; they are kin-grade attachments that he tends actively — calls, visits, present-on-the-bad-day behavior — across years of operational chaos.

### 6.4.2 Romantic Capacity

Despite the breakup pattern (Vera, Trish), the underlying capacity is genuine and intact: he loves attentively, courts with charm, listens, sustains. The Trish Tilby relationship in particular was, while it lasted, one of the more emotionally articulate adult relationships in the X-Men record. The fact that partners have left him when his body changed is a wound on his side, not a deficit in his love-making capacity.

### 6.4.3 Social Range

He moves competently across radically different social registers: Avengers Mansion black-tie fundraisers, Xavier School student lounges, U.N. testimony, mutant-rights protests, Genoshan diplomatic meetings, late-night labs with Reed Richards or Tony Stark. The range is itself an asset — he is the X-Men's most effective ambassador in non-mutant elite contexts because he can pass through them without code-switch friction. He knows which fork, and he knows when to ignore which fork on purpose.

### 6.4.4 The Wider Scientific Network

He maintains working relationships with the broader Marvel-Earth scientific community — Richards, Stark, Pym, Banner, Connors, the various Wakandan and Atlantean scientific contacts. These are non-trivial assets the X-Men have repeatedly drawn on. He is the team's *call list*.

---

## 6.5 RESOURCE ASSETS

- **Institutional access.** Xavier School, Jean Grey School, X-Factor's corporate-front facilities, Avengers Mansion (alumnus standing, residual access), Krakoa-era resources, Brand Corporation history. Across his career he has rarely been long without a fully equipped laboratory and rarely without institutional cover.
- **Equipment fluency.** He does not merely use the team's high-end hardware; he *built or upgraded* much of it. Cerebro iterations, the Blackbird airframes, X-Factor's containment systems, the time-displacement rig. The asset is that the equipment around him is implicitly *his* — he can repair, repurpose, and bypass it at need.
- **Financial sufficiency.** Avengers stipends, academic and consulting income (genuine peer-reviewed work under his own and pseudonymous names), tenured-equivalent institutional support. He has never been money-precarious, which removes an entire failure mode that constrains other operators.
- **Public credibility (intermittently).** When he is in good odor with the press — the Avengers years, segments of the X-Factor public-facing period — he is one of the very few mutants treated as a *public intellectual* in mainstream media. This is a soft-power asset the team has cashed repeatedly.

---

## 6.6 RESILIENCE FACTORS — WHY THE STRUCTURE HOLDS AS LONG AS IT DOES

The defensive scaffolding that eventually fails him was, for decades, an extraordinarily *effective* resilience apparatus. The file must give it credit on its own terms.

### 6.6.1 Early-Attachment Substrate

Norton and Edna McCoy did the foundational work. The subject entered adolescence with the basic experience of *being loved as he was* by the two people whose love most mattered. This is the bedrock under everything else. Without it the visible congenital mutation would have produced a far worse adult outcome — likely the schizoid or paranoid presentation he conspicuously does *not* have. The parental bond bought him, in clinical terms, the *capacity to form adult attachments at all*, and that capacity is the substrate of every relational asset listed above.

### 6.6.2 Dual-Track Compensation (Athletics + Intellect)

The childhood adaptation — high-school football star *and* academic prodigy — gave him two independent sources of self-worth, which is unusually robust. Most gifted children armor on one track and shatter when that track fails. He could lose a game and still be the smartest kid in the room; he could lose an argument and still be the strongest. The dual track is also why his adult identity tolerates the constant body-changes as long as it does: the *mind* keeps holding up the self-image when the *body* keeps mutating out from under him.

### 6.6.3 Humor as Pressure Valve

For roughly four decades, the self-deprecating wit functions as designed — it discharges social tension before it becomes corrosive, it disarms hostile interlocutors, and it gives the subject a tolerable distance from his own appearance. It is genuinely funny, which matters; insincere humor does not regulate affect. The wit is also *generous* in its early-to-middle form — directed at himself rather than at others, inviting laughter with rather than at. This is a mature defense and it does mature work.

### 6.6.4 Sublimation Engine

The capacity to convert distress into productive output is, on the positive ledger, an immense asset. Most of the canonical scientific contributions on his record were produced under emotional load — post-Jean's death, post-Trish, post-Decimation. The engine is real and it is generative. The Endangered Species globe-spanning quest, even though it ended in moral compromise, *was* a feat of sustained sublimated grief that no one else on the team could have attempted.

### 6.6.5 Cognitive Flexibility Around Identity

The subject has been gray, blue, lupine, leonine, near-human, and several gradations between, and he has *re-integrated each form into a continuous self*. This is a rare and valuable capacity. People in the wider human population who undergo far smaller bodily changes (illness, disfigurement, aging) frequently cannot do this. He can. The public coming-out-and-retraction episode in the *New X-Men* era is another instance of the same capacity — he can *play* with identity categories as instruments because his core self is, in fact, stable enough to do so without dissociation.

### 6.6.6 Physical Courage as Baseline

He shows up. Across sixty years and hundreds of engagements, the record contains essentially no instance of the subject failing to enter a fight he was needed in, including fights he expected to lose, fights against opponents far outside his weight class, and fights in which his own life was the likely cost. Courage in him is not effortful; it is dispositional. This is a resilience asset because it removes the *should I act* anxiety that paralyzes lesser operators and lets cognition focus on *how*.

### 6.6.7 Vocational Anchor

Across every era — original X-Men, Avengers, X-Factor, Jean Grey School, Krakoa — he has had *work he believed in*. The vocational continuity is itself a stabilizer. He has never been adrift without role, which is a known protective factor against the worst outcomes for high-IQ individuals with personality vulnerabilities.

### 6.6.8 The Capacity for Genuine Guilt

Paradoxically listed under strengths: the subject *feels* the wrong he does. This is precisely why the rationalization engine has to work so hard in the late period — there is a conscience underneath it that will not quietly die. A man without that conscience would not need the elaborate justifications; he would simply act. The presence of the guilt is the residual asset that makes a recovery arc, at any post-execution resurrection point, *possible*. The earlier-self resurrection that replaced the Krakoan version is in-universe evidence that the institution believes the core moral material is salvageable. It would not be salvageable in a true sociopath. It is salvageable in him.

---

## 6.7 META-ASSETS — WHAT MAKES THE LEDGER DURABLE

Three structural features make the above assets unusually persistent against decay:

1. **Redundancy.** No single failure point collapses him. Lose the body to mutation? The mind holds. Lose a relationship? The friend network holds. Lose the institution? The vocational identity holds. This redundancy is the deep reason he has survived sixty years of events that retired or destroyed lesser figures.

2. **Self-repairing social capital.** His friendships are *low-maintenance and high-trust*, which means that years of operational separation do not degrade them. Bobby Drake re-engages instantly across any gap. Wonder Man does the same. This is a kind of relational compound interest that most adults do not accumulate.

3. **The teaching reflex.** Even at his worst, he transmits knowledge. The Krakoa-era spymaster who was doing terrible things was *simultaneously* mentoring students. The reflex outlives the ethics. This matters because it means the institutional value he produces continues to accrue even during his own decompensation — and because, on recovery, the channel through which he re-enters the moral community is already open.

---

## 6.8 SUMMARY FINDING — POSITIVE LEDGER

The subject is, even after the most damning entries elsewhere in this file are weighed, **a net asset of historic magnitude to the institution and to the wider mutant and human communities**. The intellect is genuinely apex; the body is a tier-one combat and survival platform; the relational capacity is rare and deep; the courage and vocational commitment are unwavering; the resilience scaffolding has absorbed more than perhaps any comparable figure in the record and continued to produce. The collapse documented in Sections 1, 3, and 4 is real and must be understood as such — but the materials from which a restored Henry McCoy can be built are, as the in-universe replacement decision implicitly concedes, *still present in the file*. The positive ledger is not a balance sheet against the negative; it is the substrate the negative grew out of and the substrate any future repair will use. The same architecture that, under sustained moral injury, generates the rationalization engine is, under healthier conditions, the architecture of one of the most consequential intellects and most reliable friends in the entire X-canon. The file's working judgment is that the assets are not merely greater than the liabilities — they are, properly handled, *the means by which the liabilities can be resolved*.


## Failure Modes & Decompensation

# FAILURE MODES & DECOMPENSATION

*Section 7 of the Henry Philip McCoy intelligence workup. Cross-reference Sections 3 (Psychological) and 4 (Psychiatric). This section maps the staged sequence by which a stable, high-functioning subject converts under load into the late-period operator the canon documents; identifies the precise environmental and internal conditions that initiate and accelerate each stage; and specifies the observable behavioral, somatic, linguistic, and operational tells at each waypoint.*

---

## 7.0 Threshold Statement

Subject does not fail in the manner of most catastrophically-decompensating peers. He does not rage (cf. Logan), does not dissociate into alternate personality (cf. Jean), does not collapse into substance (cf. Tony Stark), does not retreat into catatonic withdrawal. There is no single rupture event in his record. His failure is **slow, articulate, and reasoned in clean prose at every step**. This is the central forensic difficulty with the subject: his decompensation looks, from the inside and often from the outside, like *increased competence applied to harder problems*. The decompensation IS the competence, escalating past the point where the underlying ethical and affective systems can throttle it.

The collapse pattern is therefore best modeled not as a breakdown but as a **disinhibition cascade** in which each successive defense, deployed in good faith, removes a brake the prior version of the subject relied upon. By the terminus the only remaining brake is external — peer action — which is in fact what the canon delivers.

---

## 7.1 The Six-Stage Escalation Path

The longitudinal record (1963–present) supports a six-stage model. Stages 1–3 are recoverable and recur multiple times across his life as transient stress responses. Stages 4–6 are observed only in the late period (post-2005) and, once entered, the record shows no spontaneous return to baseline without external intervention.

### Stage 1 — Verbal Densification

The earliest and most reliable tell. Under any meaningful stressor — physical danger, relational injury, news of a peer's death, a failed experiment — subject's diction escalates. Sentence length increases. Latinate vocabulary displaces Anglo-Saxon. Allusive density rises: a Stage-0 baseline utterance might reference one author or concept per paragraph; Stage-1 produces three to five. Subordinate clauses proliferate. Self-reference shifts from first-person direct ("I think") to first-person ironized ("one supposes," "your humble narrator submits," "the present subject is forced to conclude").

This is observable in the record across every era: the X-Mansion infirmary scenes following Jean's death in *Uncanny X-Men* #137, post-Infectia dialogues, the early Endangered Species monologues. Latency from stressor to Stage 1: minutes to hours. Cost to subject: minimal. Recovery: spontaneous, usually within 24–72 hours of stressor resolution. **Stage 1 is, properly understood, the subject functioning within design tolerance.** It becomes diagnostic only when sustained beyond a week without de-escalation, which signals progression to Stage 2.

### Stage 2 — Lab Withdrawal & Sleep Compression

When Stage 1 fails to discharge the stressor, subject enters the lab. Behavioral correlates: 30+ hour work cycles, meals taken at the bench, sleep compressed to 2–4 hour windows of microsleep in chair or on cot, grooming neglected (anomalous for the subject, who is normally meticulous about the fur — see Section 6, Habits & Tics). Verbal output decreases in volume but Stage-1 density persists; conversation becomes terse-but-still-ornate, a curious register specific to him.

Social withdrawal in Stage 2 is selective rather than total. He continues to answer Bobby Drake. He will field one Jean Grey query. He will not respond to administrative communications, students, or romantic partners. Trish Tilby's complaints across the late-80s record map cleanly onto Stage-2 patterns. Vera Cantor experienced earlier, milder versions.

The functional purpose of Stage 2 is **sublimation under containment**: the stressor is converted into productive output, the body is punished into compliance with the cognitive demand, and affective processing is delayed indefinitely. The cost is that affect does not actually dissipate; it queues. Subjects with this defensive structure characteristically discover, weeks or months later, that they are grieving or furious about something they believed they had handled. The subject's record contains multiple instances of delayed-affect surfacing (the eventual breakdown about Jean during the X-Factor era; the late-coming recognition of what Trish's departure actually meant).

Recovery from Stage 2: requires either external interruption (Bobby is historically the most effective interrupter) or the completion of a substantive piece of work that the subject can present as restitution for whatever the stressor was. Without one of these, progression to Stage 3 within two to six weeks.

### Stage 3 — Closed-Loop Ethical Reasoning

The hinge stage. The point at which subject's decompensation becomes *generative of bad action* rather than merely costly to himself.

Tell: he begins to argue ethics out loud, in extended monologue, to audiences who did not ask. The arguments are syllogistically clean. They invariably conclude with a recommendation for action that he has, in fact, already decided to take. The reasoning is post-hoc but presented as deliberation. He is at this stage soliciting agreement, not input — a distinction his interlocutors usually recognize within two or three exchanges.

Linguistic markers specific to Stage 3: increased use of *we* where he means *I* ("we cannot allow," "we must consider," delivered when no consultation has occurred); rising frequency of moral-load words deployed in clinical register ("unconscionable," "intolerable," "morally indefensible") applied to the inaction option rather than to the proposed action; appearance of preemptive concession ("I am aware how this will sound, but…") which functions to disarm objection rather than to invite it.

In the early record, Stage 3 was throttled by Xavier, by Jean, by Scott in his pre-Schism mode. The throttling worked because subject still privately recognized those individuals as ethical authorities. Across the post-2005 record the available throttlers diminish (Jean dead, Xavier's authority shattered by his secret manipulations, Scott estranged), and the closed loop closes. By the time of the *All-New X-Men* time-travel decision, every relevant peer is on record opposing the action; he proceeds.

Stage 3 is the last stage at which **internal correction remains possible**. Beyond it, the rationalization engine has eaten the conscience function it was meant to serve.

### Stage 4 — Unilateral Action Under Ethical Cover

Action is taken. The action is large. It is taken without consent of those it affects and often without disclosure to those whose authority it bypasses. Concurrent with the action, subject produces — usually in expository monologue or journal entry — a finished ethical justification that he believes to be airtight.

The Endangered Species solicitations of Sinister and the High Evolutionary are Stage 4. The retrieval of the original five are Stage 4. The early Krakoan X-Force operations are Stage 4. The pattern: an act that the subject's Stage-0 self would have refused outright is executed with full deliberation and zero affective alarm.

Diagnostic feature of Stage 4: **the absence of guilt is itself novel and notable**. Subject's Stage-0 baseline includes pronounced guilt response — he is by temperament scrupulous, and minor ethical lapses (a sharp remark to a student, a missed obligation to Trish) generate disproportionate self-reproach for days. In Stage 4 he commits acts orders of magnitude more serious without observable internal disturbance. The disturbance has not vanished; it has been *bracketed* by the rationalization, parked outside the operational frame. It will return, with interest, only at Stage 6.

Recovery from Stage 4 without external intervention has not been observed in the late-period record.

### Stage 5 — Instrumentalization of Allies

The escalation pattern's qualitative shift. Up through Stage 4 subject's victims are abstract or adversarial — the genetic future, hostile foreign states, criminal networks. At Stage 5 the calculation extends to *people on his own side*.

The serial resurrection and operational abuse of Colossus during the Krakoan X-Force run is the cleanest instance. Stranding the time-displaced teens for years past the point at which return was viable is another. The pattern: an ally is treated as a resource to be allocated against an objective, with the moral weight of their personhood discounted to whatever the calculation requires.

Subject at Stage 5 retains surface warmth toward the instrumentalized ally. He is not cold, not contemptuous, not dismissive — these would be tells he would notice in himself. He is *warm and using them anyway*. This is the late-period configuration that most disturbs his peers when they reconstruct events, because it indicates the defensive structure has compromised not just his judgment but his perception of what relationship is.

Tells at Stage 5: ledger-language about people ("acceptable cost," "operational asset," "necessary attrition") slipped into otherwise normal dialogue; planning sessions in which he refuses to brief the affected party on the role they will play; an emergent pattern of compartmentalization in which different allies receive different versions of the same operation.

### Stage 6 — Defense of the Defensive Structure Itself

Terminal stage in the observed record. Reached only when allies have begun to confront him directly with the cumulative pattern. The decompensation here is the subject's response *to being correctly named*.

Stage-6 behavior: dismissal of accusers' standing to judge; reframing of their objection as failure of nerve or imagination; assertion that they would, in his place, do the same and only their unwillingness to bear the weight prevents them; in extremis, willingness to act *against* the accusers to protect the operational structure. The defensive perimeter, having absorbed conscience itself, now extends to anyone threatening to restore conscience from outside.

The canon's resolution — execution by his peers and replacement by an earlier-resurrection self — is the documented terminus. It is worth stating plainly: **the subject's defensive structure, at full extension, was incompatible with continued existence in the social world it had been built to navigate**. The system around him had to remove him because nothing he could do from inside himself could.

---

## 7.2 What His Collapse Looks Like (Phenomenology)

To an observer with access to the subject across time, the late-period collapse does not present as collapse. It presents as:

- A man who **still looks the same** — same grooming, same dressing-gown elegance in the lab, same purring chuckle, same Wilde quotation at the threshold of every difficult conversation.
- Whose **work output has, if anything, increased** — more papers, more inventions, more operational successes, more lives saved by direct intervention.
- Whose **social calendar remains active** — opera dates, faculty dinners, the long-standing chess game with Bobby — though attendance grows erratic and lateness, formerly anomalous, becomes routine.
- Whose **decisions, examined in isolation, each have a defensible rationale** — and whose decisions, examined in sequence over eighteen months, describe a trajectory no Stage-0 version of the subject would have endorsed.
- Whose **conversations with longtime intimates** acquire a faint quality of performance — as if he is doing an impression of himself, very accurately, from memory.

The last is the most reliable observer signal and the hardest to formalize. Bobby Drake, the most attuned witness across the canon, is on record across multiple late-period arcs registering precisely this: that Hank sounds like Hank, looks like Hank, but is producing the Hank-signal rather than emitting it natively.

Somatic correlates at full decompensation: the secondary-mutation features intensify under stress — pupils slit more visibly, the purr-growl becomes more frequent and at lower thresholds, the canines show more in speech. He grooms more, not less; the fur is immaculate in periods when his ethics are most compromised. The body, in other words, **announces the disinhibition that his speech is at pains to conceal**. A trained observer reading the somatics rather than the diction would detect Stage 4 months before the dialogue gave it away.

---

## 7.3 Conditions That Produce Decompensation

The escalation does not initiate spontaneously. The record permits identification of specific conditions that, in combination, reliably trigger it.

**Necessary conditions (must be present):**

- **A problem he believes only he can solve.** Decompensation requires a stressor that engages the core self-concept (*indispensable mind in service of survival*). Routine danger does not trigger it; he handles routine danger as well as anyone on the roster. Existential-stakes problems with no obviously qualified peer are required.
- **Time pressure with no natural deliberative pause.** Decimation, the terminal-illness window, the Krakoan operational tempo — all share the quality that *stopping to consult* is framed (by him, by circumstance, or both) as itself a moral failure. The architecture relies on pause for self-correction; remove pause and the architecture fails.

**Sufficient accelerants (any one rapidly advances stage):**

- **Loss of a primary ethical interlocutor.** Jean Grey's deaths, Xavier's exposure as compromised, the rupture with Scott. Each removal of someone whose ethical authority he privately respected widened the closed loop.
- **Bodily betrayal.** Each new mutation (secondary, tertiary) preceded a major decompensation episode. The body announces it is not in his control; the response is to assert control somewhere else, harder.
- **Romantic loss tied to appearance.** The Trish Tilby departure pattern, when it recurs (and its echoes recur with other partners), reactivates the founding wound and increases compensatory pressure.
- **Public framing of him as monstrous.** Anti-mutant press cycles, accusations from teammates that he is "becoming what he opposes." Counter-intuitively these *accelerate* rather than arrest the slide — the defensive structure cannot metabolize the accusation, so it must be denied via further action that proves the accusation wrong (and which, of course, proves it right).

**Protective conditions (presence prevents or reverses decompensation):**

- **An active dyad with Bobby Drake.** The single most reliable throttle in the record. Bobby's specific gift is that he registers Stage 1 in real time and *names* it, in their private vernacular, before Stage 2 sets in. When Bobby is present, available, and on speaking terms, the subject rarely progresses past Stage 2.
- **A teaching load.** Direct contact with students appears to engage some affective circuit the lab work bypasses. Periods of intensive Jean Grey School involvement correlate with the longest stretches of stability.
- **A substantive piece of work the subject can finish.** Completion discharges the queue. Open-ended, perpetually-deferred missions (Endangered Species; the Krakoan intelligence apparatus) are the inverse — they maintain the disinhibited operational state indefinitely.
- **Pre-fur intimacy.** Time with anyone who knew him before *Amazing Adventures* #11 — Bobby, Warren, Scott when reachable — appears to re-ground self-concept. The record shows him deliberately seeking these contacts during early-stage stress, and conspicuously avoiding them during Stage 4+.

---

## 7.4 What He Would Need To Recover (Were Recovery Available)

The structural answer: **a forced, sustained pause in which affect is permitted to surface without an immediate sublimating outlet, conducted in the presence of an interlocutor whose ethical authority he cannot dismiss, with no problem available to solve.** None of these conditions has ever been engineered for him in the canon. Each is, individually, contrary to his preference and his self-image; in combination they would require captivity, which his peers were unwilling to impose until the terminus, at which point they chose execution-and-replacement instead.

It is worth registering this as the system-level failure the record actually documents. The subject's decompensation is treatable in principle. The treatment was never available because no institution he belonged to was structured to deliver it, and his own defensive structure was specifically optimized to refuse it. The canon's resolution is not justice; it is the cheapest available substitute for a kind of care his world did not know how to provide.

---

## 7.5 Summary Forensic Read

The subject fails in the manner his defenses were built to prevent failure: invisibly, articulately, and at increasing operational tempo. The collapse does not present as collapse because at every stage the subject can produce a plausible account of why the current behavior is the correct application of his lifelong principles to a uniquely-difficult problem. The accounts are, taken one at a time, often persuasive. Taken in sequence over the late-period record, they describe a man whose rationalization function has metastasized into the entire ethical apparatus, leaving no internal organ capable of registering when he has gone wrong. The collapse, in short, is **conscience eaten by its own most successful defense**, with the body announcing the catastrophe in slit pupils and rising purr-rate while the voice continues to quote Byron in perfect meter.


## Trajectory & Forward Assessment

# UATU ANALYTICAL WORKUP: HENRY PHILIP McCOY ("BEAST")
## Section 6 — Trajectory & Forward Assessment

*Where the subject is going, and what could bend the curve. All projections derive from sixty years of behavioral evidence summarized in Sections 1–5; the discipline of this section is to extrapolate without inventing.*

---

### 6.1 The Structural Problem That Defines the Forecast

Any prognosis for this subject begins with a single, awkward in-universe fact: he has already been killed by his closest colleagues and replaced with an earlier-resurrection iteration of himself. That is not a footnote. It is the most consequential data point we possess about his trajectory, and it must be read in two registers simultaneously.

In the **first register** (what literally happened), the late-period subject was excised — a person his peers concluded could not be corrected from within, only ended and overwritten. In the **second register** (what the excision *does not solve*), the replacement Hank carries the same congenital architecture, the same childhood, the same defensive scaffolding, the same OCP-trending-toward-compensatory-narcissism structure that produced the executed Hank in the first place. The *contents* of memory differ; the *engine* does not. Forecasting his future means forecasting what that engine, restarted at an earlier point on its own trajectory, will and will not do differently when subjected to comparable loads.

The honest baseline projection is therefore not "he has been reset." It is: **he has been given one more pass through the same gradient, with the partial gift of knowing — at some level, even if only as inherited reputation — that the gradient terminates badly.** Whether that knowledge functions as a brake or as a fresh source of shame to be defended against is the central open question of his remaining life.

---

### 6.2 The Five-Year Horizon (Short-Term Trajectory)

In the immediate aftermath of his return-as-earlier-self, several behaviors are predictable with high confidence:

- **Performative penitence.** Expect a sustained period of conspicuous moral modesty: deferral to teammates on tactical calls, ostentatious requests for second opinions in the lab, a willingness to be wrong out loud. This will be partly genuine and partly *another performance of the self he wishes to be seen as*. The diagnostic question is whether the modesty survives the first crisis that he believes only he can solve. Historical base-rate says: it will hold for the first crisis, soften at the second, and disappear at the third.
- **Compulsive reading-into-the-record.** He will study what his prior iteration did the way a man reads his own autopsy. He is constitutionally incapable of *not* knowing. He will sit alone with the files of Krakoan operations, of the Terra Verde coup, of what was done to Colossus, and he will metabolize them through intellectualization — the exact defense that produced the harm to begin with. Watch for the moment he begins constructing an *explanation* for the prior Hank's behavior that subtly exonerates the underlying defensive structure. ("He was dying." "He was under Krakoan duress." "The geopolitics required…") Every clause of exoneration is a forecast of recurrence.
- **Re-anchoring to vetted dyads.** He will move quickly to reconstitute his oldest, most-trusted relationships — Bobby Drake first, then the surviving original-five circle, then Wonder Man if available, then his most reliable scientific peers. These are the people in front of whom he is least defended and most correctable. Their proximity is a protective factor; their absence or alienation would be a leading indicator of relapse.
- **Lab return.** Sublimation will reassert quickly. Within months expect 30-hour cycles, multiple parallel projects, a public-facing project (teaching, the Jean Grey School successor framework) and one or two quieter ones whose scope he downplays. The quiet projects are the ones to watch.

The five-year window is, on balance, **the safest period of his remaining life.** The shame of what was done in his name is fresh, the watchfulness of his peers is high, and his own architecture is, for the moment, oriented toward repair rather than expansion. This is also the window in which intervention is most viable.

---

### 6.3 The Mid-Range Horizon (Five to Twenty Years)

This is where the forecast bifurcates, and where the *fork points* live.

The mid-range is the period during which all of his prior catastrophes incubated. Endangered Species did not happen in week one of Decimation; it took years of accumulated failure to produce the willingness to call on Sinister. The Krakoan spymaster role did not arrive at island-founding; it arrived after the institution had stabilized and the *invisibility of intelligence work* became a permission structure. The pattern is consistent: **Hank's worst decisions are not panic responses; they are the cooled-down residue of a long period during which a problem he could not solve sat in his peripheral vision until he decided it had become his personal responsibility.**

Mid-range fork points, in order of probability:

**Fork A — A second existential threat to mutantkind (or to a population he identifies with).** Extremely likely on a twenty-year horizon; it is the recurring weather of his world. The diagnostic question is not *whether* it happens but *what he does in year three of it*, when consensus solutions have plateaued and his teammates are exhausted. This is the exact ecological niche in which his rationalization engine reignites. Protective factor: a peer or partner with explicit, pre-agreed veto authority over his unilateral actions. Risk factor: any framework — Krakoan, post-Krakoan, or successor — that grants him intelligence-portfolio responsibility without external audit. **He must never again be the man who decides in private what is necessary.** Any institution that drifts him back into that role is, on the evidence, fatal to him.

**Fork B — A new bodily transformation.** Statistically likely; his mutation has demonstrated a pattern of approximately decadal drift. A *quaternary* morphologic shift would be the most psychologically destabilizing event possible for him, because it would reopen the central wound (the body that will not stay) at a point in life when the compensatory architecture is already known to fail. Critical sub-question: would such a transformation move him *toward* the human silhouette or *further* from it? Toward-human would be in some ways more destabilizing, because it would invite a fantasy of restoration he has spent his life refusing to permit himself. Further-from-human would feed the dysmorphic substrate directly. There is no benign version of this event; there are only versions he is and is not prepared for. Preparation is achievable only via the work named in 6.5.

**Fork C — Mortality, his own.** He has been told he was dying once and made his worst decision in response. If he is told he is dying again — and given his self-experimentation history and his exposure profile, the probability over twenty years is non-trivial — the prior response is the base rate. Protective factor: prior witnessing of what *terminal-Hank* did. Risk factor: the specific psychology of "this time I will do it *correctly*," which is precisely the form rationalization takes in a man who has already been wrong once.

**Fork D — Mortality, of an anchor relationship.** Loss of Bobby Drake, of Jean, of Wonder Man, of any of the small set of people in front of whom he is least defended, would remove a structural brake. Grief in this subject is metabolized through work; work in this subject historically scales into unilateral world-saving. The death of an anchor is, paradoxically, more dangerous than his own.

**Fork E — A confrontation with his Krakoan victims.** Colossus, the surviving citizenry of Terra Verde, the time-displaced teens (or their adult selves). Whether and how this confrontation happens — whether he is permitted to apologize, whether the apology is accepted, whether he is required to *make material restitution rather than verbal* — is one of the single largest variables in his long-range outcome. A purely verbal reckoning, processed through his native intellectualization, will not metabolize. A required years-long restitutional labor (medical, reconstructive, civic) would be the closest available analog to genuine integration. This is the intervention with the highest expected value; it is also the one his defenses will work hardest to convert into something more comfortable.

---

### 6.4 The Long Horizon (Twenty Years and Beyond)

On a long enough timeline, two outcomes dominate the probability mass.

**Outcome 1 — The elder-statesman integration.** Plausible but not default. In this outcome, the work of the next five years takes; the mid-range fork points are navigated with peer accompaniment rather than alone; the moral injuries of the prior iteration are metabolized into a chastened, durable, *teaching* posture. The man becomes what Xavier was supposed to become and never quite did: a moral authority whose authority derives in part from public, owned failure. Pedagogically this version is invaluable; his students would inherit not the brilliance (which cannot be taught) but the *discipline of self-mistrust* (which can). This Hank ends his life as the X-Men's institutional conscience — not because he is most ethical, but because he is the one who knows most precisely how ethics fails from the inside.

**Outcome 2 — The slow re-escalation.** The default. In this outcome, the early modesty fades by the third crisis; the rationalization engine reboots more cautiously this time, but reboots; the unilateralism re-emerges in subtler forms (advisory rather than operational, influence rather than command); and somewhere in the third or fourth decade he commits, again, an act that his peers find unforgivable. The act is smaller than the prior one — that is the form learning takes in a defensive structure that has not been dismantled, only restrained — but it is recognizably the same class of act. He is not executed this time; he is *retired*, quietly, by people who love him and do not trust him. He dies in a study surrounded by books, having outlived several of the people whose absence will have helped to undo him.

Between these two outcomes, a third, less probable but worth naming: **Outcome 3 — the late catastrophic act.** Low probability but high consequence. If forks B and C arrive in close succession (a new transformation followed by terminal diagnosis, or vice versa), the architecture's failure mode is no longer slow re-escalation but rapid moral disinhibition under existential framing, exactly as in the *All-New X-Men* decision. The act this time would not be time-travel; it would be whatever his late-period intellect identifies as the *most leveraged* single intervention available — likely something at the genetic or temporal substrate of mutantkind itself, on a scale that makes the prior unilateralism look local. This outcome is what his peers must be most vigilant against in the final quarter of his life, and what he himself, in his best moments, must learn to name and forbid in advance.

---

### 6.5 What Would Push Him Toward Growth

The protective interventions are specific and they are not the ones he would design for himself. (He would design more reading, more journaling, more eloquent self-examination. These are the disease wearing the costume of the cure.)

- **Required somatic practice, non-verbal.** Anything that returns him to the body as *inhabitant* rather than as *commentator*: martial discipline under a teacher he cannot out-reason, sustained physical labor with no scientific yield, contemplative practice that forbids language. He has spent sixty years escaping the body upward into language; the corrective is the slow re-occupancy of the body without the language.
- **A standing veto.** A person — ideally two, ideally including one who is not a mutant and not a scientist — with pre-agreed, publicly acknowledged authority to halt any project of his on the basis of *concern* rather than *argument*. Argument he will win. Concern, if he has consented to honor it, he cannot dismiss without exposing the structure to himself. Bobby Drake is the obvious first candidate; he has been, across the canon, the relationship in which Hank is least able to perform.
- **Restitutional rather than expiatory labor.** As above (Fork E). Years of unglamorous, concrete, body-on-the-line repair of the specific damage done in his name. Not symposia about it. Not papers about it. The hands doing the work the hands previously did the harm with.
- **A pedagogical posture that requires admitting the worst out loud, repeatedly, to students.** Teaching is already protective for him; teaching *as a confessed cautionary instance* would be transformative. The risk is that he turns the confession into a polished set-piece. The corrective is a teaching partner who will tell him when the set-piece has gotten too smooth.
- **Therapeutic relationship with a clinician he cannot impress.** Whether this exists in his world is uncertain. If it can be arranged — and if the clinician is sufficiently armored against his verbal performance — it is the single highest-yield intervention available. The clinician's only useful question, asked repeatedly, is some form of: *What are you not saying right now, in plain words, that you are saying right now in elaborate ones?*
- **Sustained romantic partnership with a partner who has seen the worst and stayed.** The historical pattern of partners departing at the threshold of his bodily change has reinforced the central wound. A partnership that holds across a transformation — that holds *because of* rather than *despite* — would be reparative in a way nothing else available to him is. This is largely outside his control; it can only be reported as a forecastable protective factor if it occurs.

---

### 6.6 What Would Push Him Toward Catastrophe

The accelerants are equally specific.

- **Reinstatement to an intelligence or covert-operations role.** Under any institutional banner, with any oversight regime he believes himself smarter than. This is the loaded chamber. It must remain unloaded.
- **Isolation from the original-five anchor circle.** Through death, estrangement, or geographic separation. The further from those witnesses he drifts, the freer the rationalization engine runs.
- **A peer publicly humiliating him intellectually.** Especially in a domain he considers his own. The wound to his self-concept here is asymmetric to the offense, and his response would be the cold, planned, multi-year kind.
- **A framing of an emergent crisis as soluble only by him.** Whether the framing comes from outside (manipulation) or inside (the rationalization engine in flattering mode), this is the trigger configuration his architecture is least equipped to refuse.
