- **Access to substrates of unusual leverage** — temporal, genetic, reality-altering — *without* a standing veto in place. He should not be near such tools alone. Not because he is malicious; because his ethical brake is structurally affective and his affect is structurally isolated, and the brake therefore fails precisely where the leverage is highest.
- **A new terminal diagnosis with no witnesses to his prior terminal-diagnosis behavior.** The combination is the worst-case input to the system.

---

### 6.7 The Open Questions

Several variables cannot be resolved from the available evidence and will determine which outcome obtains:

1. **Does the replacement iteration carry the prior iteration's memories in any operative form?** If yes, the shame is a resource and a hazard. If no, the lesson must be reconstructed externally and may not take.
2. **Will the institutions around him recognize that the structural problem is the structure, not the contents?** If they treat the prior execution as having solved the problem, they will reload the chamber within a decade.
3. **Will he ever submit to a discipline he cannot out-talk?** Every protective intervention listed above depends on this. It is the single largest unknown about his remaining life.
4. **What does he do the first time he is, again, certainly right and certainly alone in being right?** Because that situation will arise. The whole forecast turns on whether he has, by then, internalized that *being right is not authorization to act unilaterally* — a proposition his entire life has trained him to disbelieve.
5. **Is there, anywhere in his world, a person who loves him and is not impressed by him?** This person is the rarest and most necessary resource. If such a person exists and remains in his life, the prognosis is meaningfully better. If not, the architecture will eventually run unopposed.

---

### 6.8 Forecast Summary

On the evidence, the modal outcome is the slow re-escalation — a quieter, more chastened recurrence of the same pattern, terminating in retirement rather than execution, somewhere in the fourth decade from now. The elder-statesman integration is achievable but requires interventions his defenses will resist and his institutions are unlikely to impose. The late catastrophic act is low-probability but must be planned against, because its consequences would dwarf everything in the prior record.

The tragedy already legible in the seventeen-year-old quoting Byron is not yet fully written. There is a version of his remaining life in which the boy who armored a real shame in real brilliance learns, late, to set the armor down in front of two or three people and discover that the body underneath is, after all these decades, acceptable. That version is available. It is not the default. It will require him to do the one thing his entire defensive architecture was built to make unnecessary: to be known, in plain language, without performance, by someone he cannot out-think.

Whether he does this is the file's last open question, and the one the next sixty years will answer.

*— End Section 6. Continue to Section 7: Operational Recommendations.*

## Relationship Graph
### Bobby Drake
- Oldest dyadic anchor; the friendship that predates the fur
- Primary reach-vector - Bobby is one of the few who can interrupt the syllogism
- Failure mode: Bobby's emotional directness reads to Hank as unsophistication; if Hank decides Bobby 'doesn't see the bigger picture,' the bond is bypassed rather than broken, and the bypass is the warning that Stage 3 is imminent

### [[Jean Grey-Summers (Marvel Girl / Phoenix / Dark Phoenix / White Phoenix of the Crown)]]
- Conscience-channel; pre-fur witness; one of two people whose disappointment he cannot rationalize away in real time
- Failure mode: Jean's death (or absence) removes a critical brake; his worst decisions historically cluster around periods when she is dead or unavailable
- Leverage: a credible appeal in Jean's voice or memory will at least pause him

### Wonder Man
- Avengers-era best friend; the relationship in which Hank was happiest and most extroverted
- Decompression bond - Simon is the one person around whom Hank does not have to be useful
- Failure mode: dormant in the X-Men-centric periods; Hank loses access to the version of himself who could simply enjoy a cocktail and an opera, and the loss compounds the compensatory drift

### Trish Tilby
- Closed wound; the partner whose recoil from the secondary mutation confirmed the body-shame thesis
- Failure mode (already realized): exit over the body. Leaves a template Hank applies preemptively to every subsequent romantic possibility
- Leverage: invoking her is cruel and effective; do not use lightly

### Abigail Brand
- Peer-intellect partnership; S.W.O.R.D. liaison; one of the few romantic/professional bonds where his mind, not his body, is the operating currency
- Failure mode: shared comfort with morally gray operational decisions can accelerate rather than restrain his unilateralism - they enable each other's calculus

### [[Scott Summers (Cyclops)]]
- Estranged since Schism; mutual disappointment hardened into mutual contempt
- Failure mode (already realized): Hank's time-travel decision was explicitly weaponized against Scott; the relationship is now adversarial-with-history
- Leverage: framing a request as 'unlike Scott' resonates; framing it as 'like Scott' inflames

### [[James Howlett (Logan / Wolverine / Patch / Weapon X / Death)]]
- Jean Grey School co-founder, operational ally through the Wolverine-aligned period
- Failure mode: Logan's pragmatic violence gave Hank permission structures for his own, and Hank rationalized further than Logan would have endorsed
- Leverage: Logan as a check is effective in person, ineffective at distance

### [[Charles Francis Xavier (Professor X)]]
- Deceased mentor; internalized model of benevolent unilateralism, absorbed without checksum
- Failure mode (already realized): Hank exceeded the model. Xavier's death is the proximal trigger for the time-travel decision; the unprocessed grief and unprocessed inheritance are both load-bearing in late-period collapse

### Sinister And Dark Beast And High Evolutionary
- Compromised professional contacts from Endangered Species onward
- Failure mode (already realized): each engagement was justified, each accreted, and the cumulative compromise normalized monstrous collaborators in his Rolodex
